Blood Assassination Corps," "Assassination Bombing Corps," and others, criticizing the Chamber of Commerce for failing to persuade merchants to stop selling Japanese goods. The Chamber of Commerce immediately sent letters to various trade associations, advising them to arouse their conscience and stop selling Japanese goods. However, the Chamber of Commerce is composed of various trade associations and can only advise merchants not to sell Japanese goods, without the power to force them not to sell Japanese goods. After the September 18th Incident, various merchants organized a Merchant Voluntary Economic Boycott of Japan Committee, but because it was ineffective, it was heavily criticized by people in society and dissolved informally. Today's bomb incident was expected long ago. However, the Chamber of Commerce has no power to force those cold-blooded animals not to sell. We hope that people in society will understand our difficulties. We have already reported the bombing situation to the Municipal Government's Social Affairs Bureau, Public Security Bureau, and Municipal Party Headquarters. Today, the Public Security Bureau issued a circular to all urban and rural police districts and security teams, special task force teams, instructing them to pay attention to pedestrians in prosperous streets and lanes, deploy armed detectives at major intersections on each street, take serious precautions, and advance and extend the curfew time by one hour each night. The Second Army Headquarters also ordered the Tianjin Gendarmerie Team to cooperate with the Security Team in conducting serious patrols. If such incidents occur again in the future, the relevant personnel will be held accountable and severely punished by the police and gendarmerie.

Since the September 18th Incident, former Mayor Zhang Xueming and current Mayor Zhou Longguang have repeatedly suppressed the patriotic movements of the people. On the 14th of this month, a box of Mid-Autumn Festival gifts was sent to Mayor Zhou by mail. The place of posting was No. 200, Neiwubu Street, Beijing, Iron Residence Sealed. It was opened by Section Chief Mu Daohou, with Zhou also present. Unexpectedly, the box contained a bomb. Zhou was very frightened. After investigation, the bomb was fifteen inches long and weighed fifteen pounds. After the detonator was removed and the explosives poured out and inspected, it was confirmed to be a powerful bomb. If the box had been opened carelessly at the time, there would have been a risk to life. A letter was also attached to the box, also warning not to suppress the patriotic movement any further. Recently, security at the Municipal Government has been particularly tightened. No one can enter without a pass.

After receiving reports from the Japanese Police Station and Japanese Gendarmerie Team regarding the Zhongyuan Company bomb incident, Goto, the Japanese Deputy Consul in Tianjin, believed that it was an anti-Japanese movement. In addition to reporting to the Consul General to protest to the Provincial Government, he visited Mayor Zhou Longguang at 3:00 PM on the 15th and lodged a verbal protest. Zhou refuted him, saying that the incident occurred in the Japanese Concession and that no evidence had been obtained to indicate that it was an anti-Japanese act. At 4:00 PM on the 16th, Goto went to the Municipal Government again to protest and was received by Secretary He Tingliu. Goto also stated that the bomb incidents at the Municipal Chamber of Commerce and the Chongqing Fabric Store that day were clearly anti-Japanese movements and demanded strict suppression to prevent the deterioration of Sino-Japanese relations and the occurrence of misunderstandings. Secretary He agreed to convey it to the Mayor for handling. It is reported that the Municipal Government has ordered the Public Security Bureau to issue a notice that if any acts that obstruct public order occur again in the future, those who are arrested or reported will be punished in accordance with martial law and will not be lenient.

Since the 16th, Shinsaka Kyoichi, the Chief of the Japanese Concession Police Station, who was given two major demerits due to the Zhongyuan bomb, has been strictly searching the residences of merchants and residents and inspecting pedestrians entering the Japanese Concession at each intersection between the Chinese and Japanese areas. When trams enter the Japanese Concession, they must also stop for inspection. At night, sandbags and electric wire nets are placed on Akashi Street and Fukushima Street, and armored vehicles patrol, resembling the tense situation during the Tianjin Incident last year. As a result, residents of the Japanese Concession are panicking and the market is declining. (17th)

Noulens Sentenced to Life Imprisonment 76

The Noulens Were Silent

The Jiangsu High Court tried the case of Noulens and Wang Deli for endangering the Republic of China. After more than ten court sessions, the defense concluded on the 17th, and the verdict was scheduled to be announced on the 19th. When the court session began at 9:00 AM that morning, security inside and outside the court was very tight. All spectators were searched by the police before entering the courtroom. After the judges took their seats, Noulens and Wang were brought into the court. The clerk first read the records of the 15th and 16th, which were translated by translator Yang Zhaolong. Noulens made some defenses regarding the procedures of the police opening the box for inspection and the doubts about the form of the key and the evidence, and supplemented his statements. After proper consideration, it was corrected until 12:00 noon. Chief Judge Li Mian announced that, based on all the evidence that Noulens and Wang Deli had committed crimes, the purpose was nothing more than disturbing public order, colluding with rebels, inciting the army, and disrupting discipline. It was a violation of Articles 1, 2, and 4 of the Emergency Criminal Law for Endangering the Republic of China, Articles 2 and 1 of Article 2, and Article 6, (the crime under Article 5 of the same law for which the prosecutor brought charges was declared innocent due to lack of evidence) and Article 74 of the Criminal Code of the Republic of China. They should each be sentenced to one death penalty and merged. Now, in accordance with Article 2 of the Amnesty Act, each is sentenced to life imprisonment. If the defendants are not satisfied, they can appeal to the Supreme Court within ten days after the judgment is served, and the appeal should be forwarded to this court. After the verdict was announced, Noulens and Wang Deli were silent and looked calm. They were dismissed from the court at 12:30. The main text of the judgment is as follows:

Jiangsu High Court Criminal Division No. 69 Public Notice, Case of Noulens, etc. for Endangering the Republic of China, Judgment Main text: Noulens and Wang Deli jointly disturbed public order with the purpose of endangering the Republic of China. Each is sentenced to life imprisonment and life-long deprivation of civil rights. The steel boxes (with keys), four envelopes, six yuan and eight jiao four fen, eight hundred and twenty-three US dollars, one hundred and fifty Japanese yen, and the original documents in the case of criminal evidence are all confiscated, and the rest are innocent. August 19, 21st year of the Republic of China, Liang Tongbian, Superintendent Seal, Wu Daquan, Verification,

Journey to the West (3) 78

Begging for Food with a Golden Bowl in Hand

At 4 PM on the 13th, Mr. Yang Hucheng hosted a banquet for all the members of our survey team at the Provincial Government. Due to a conflict with the opening time of the China Science Society's annual meeting, we did not go until after 5 PM. The Provincial Government is located in the center of the city and was originally the site of the former imperial Forbidden City, so it has a large area. Walking and walking again, after entering the gate and walking for several minutes, we arrived at the Great Hall where the banquet was held. The hall was built by Mr. Feng Huanzhang and is magnificent and very impressive. It can be seen that although Feng was frugal, he did not hesitate to invest in the Provincial Government, which is related to the appearance of China and foreign countries, and paid great attention to it. At that time, because we were early, we went to the city wall behind the hall to climb and look into the distance. Feng grieved over the relics of ancient people and thought about the vicissitudes of life, and could not help but sigh.

At 6 PM, someone clapped and waved from below, instructing us to come down from the wall and take our seats. So we went down the wall in single file and gathered in front of the Great Hall to take pictures. After taking pictures, we took our seats according to the positions arranged in the seating chart. Three long tables were set up in parallel lines, with Mr. Yang Hucheng in the center as the chairman. After the music started, Zhao Shouyu, Director of the Construction Department, gave a welcome speech on behalf of Yang, who was unwell. Mr. Zhao said briefly: [In the past, many people came to Shaanxi, but they came with soldiers, exploiting the people, and invading Shaanxi. This time, the members of the survey team sacrificed the prosperity of the city and came to Shaanxi, which is very backward in terms of materials, to develop Shaanxi and to open up a new life for the people of Shaanxi. Shaanxi has suffered from drought and famine for many years, and has tasted the rare suffering of the world. Although it has abundant treasures, it cannot avoid the hungry people on the road. Because they lack science and education, they abandon their goods on the ground and do not know how to collect them. As a result, the people of Shaanxi seem to be holding golden bowls and silver chopsticks in their hands, and still begging people for food. It is really pitiful:] Mr. Zhao's beautiful words, gestures and tone were all very good, and this speech won unanimous applause from all the guests. The guests who gave replies included Qian Zongyong, Director of the Longhai Railway Bureau, and Hu Shuhua. At that time, Yang Wangxi was wearing a blue crepe gown, and his demeanor was gentle and elegant. Apart from his bright and energetic eyes, it was impossible to tell that he was a soldier.

The High Price of Duck and Low Price of Chicken in Xi'an 79

On the 14th, we conducted price surveys in various parts of Xi'an. The high cost of certain items truly surprised us. For example, roast duck is six yuan per bird, Kwong Sang Hong brand fruit syrup is one yuan and forty cents per bottle, fish is three and a half yuan per pound, soda is eight cents per bottle, gasoline is ten yuan per case, and leather wine is one yuan and eighty cents per bottle. These prices made us gasp. Chicken, however, is very cheap, with four or five fat chickens costing only one yuan. Chicken eggs can be purchased for one hundred and twenty or more per yuan. Shanxi silk coal costs about two yuan and sixty cents per hundred pounds, reaching about forty-four yuan per ton, which is indeed the highest coal price in the world. It is said that coal from the mining area can be purchased for two hundred pounds per yuan, but it is transported by waterway along the Yellow River to Tongguan, then from Tongguan to Weinan, and finally from Weinan to Xi'an. Once transportation costs are added, the price of coal increases accordingly. The transportation cost between Weinan and Xi'an alone is eight cents per hundred pounds of coal. The other costs can be imagined. In addition, coal from Yaozhou costs about two yuan and eighty cents per hundred pounds. Yaozhou is in northern Shaanxi and not far from Xi'an. The coal is transported by carts. A single-horse cart is called a "set" (the same applies to other sets). A single-horse cart can carry eight hundred to nine hundred pounds of coal, a two-horse cart can carry about one thousand five hundred pounds, a three-horse cart can carry about two thousand pounds, and a four-horse cart can carry about two thousand five hundred pounds. The transportation cost is about one yuan and one dime per hundred pounds. As for coal from Hancheng, due to its poor quality, sales are not high.

From the above, it can be seen that the high price of fish and duck is due to the lack of waterways, and the high price of coal is due to inconvenient transportation. Generally speaking, if Shaanxi's waterway and transportation problems are not resolved, then the province's industry will have no hope of development. Therefore, if the Longhai Railway line can be extended to Xi'an, it will provide a lifeline for the people of Shaanxi and a stable guarantee for the development of the Northwest. We also spoke with grain merchants and obtained the following results regarding various commodity prices:

Wheat: 22 yuan per dan (approximately 250-260 catties per dan)

Barley: 26 yuan per dan (approximately 260 catties per dan)

Millet: 15 yuan per dan (approximately 260 catties per dan)

Yellow beans: 13 yuan per dan (approximately 240 catties per dan)

Oats: 7 yuan per dan (approximately 160 catties per dan)

Sesame: 20 yuan per dan (approximately 220 catties per dan)

Vegetable oil: 40 cents per catty

Flour: 25 yuan per dan (approximately 260 catties per dan)

Corn: 10 yuan per dan (approximately 230 catties per dan)

Buckwheat: 10 yuan per dan (approximately 220 catties per dan)

Mung beans: 14 yuan per dan (approximately 230 catties per dan)

Rapeseed: 30 yuan per dan (approximately 220 catties per dan)

Sorghum: 5 yuan per dan (approximately 140-150 catties per dan)

: 13 yuan per dan (approximately 220-230 catties per dan)

As for the production and sales of various grains, there are no statistics available, so we can only inquire. In terms of finance, only the Shaanxi Provincial Bank and the Bank of Communications have no plans to establish branches in Xi'an. Furthermore, because we did not have enough time, we plan to conduct further investigations upon our return.

The famous Yanchang Petroleum has not been sold to Xi'an since 1926. The reason is that the production is scarce and can only be used for nearby areas, with no surplus to enter Xi'an. In fact, even if the oil from Yanchang could be transported to Xi'an, with Yanchang being about 750 li away from Xi'an, it would take one person and one donkey 12 days to travel. The transportation cost for each case of oil would be about five yuan. Adding the cost of about five yuan per barrel, the selling price may not be able to compete with Mobil Oil. Regarding this issue, there are other experts conducting investigations. After a field visit to Yanchang, a report will be provided. (To be continued)

Local Correspondence

Songjiang 80

Robbery of a monastery in the city. The Beichan Temple, commonly known as Maqi Temple, located inside the Dongmen (East Gate), is presided over by the monk Haiming of the Fu sect. It was robbed once in the past. Unexpectedly, at around 10 o'clock the previous night, the abbot Haiming and the monks were out chanting scriptures and had not returned. Suddenly, four men wearing gray clothes arrived, claiming to be checking for deserters. They immediately produced weapons and ordered the incense keepers not to make any noise. The thugs broke into each meditation room and looted for about a quarter of an hour before leaving swaggeringly. When the abbot Haiming and the monks returned to the temple and inspected everything, the losses included more than fifty yuan in cash and clothing.

Wujiang 81

Inspection by Committee Members from the Ministry of Industry. Feng Hefa, a member of the International Trade Bureau of the Ministry of Industry, was commissioned to investigate the recent situation of industry and commerce in Jiangsu Province. He arrived in the county for investigation. On the 16th, Committee Member Feng arrived in the county from Suzhou and went to the county government, chamber of commerce, and other agencies to conduct investigations. On the 18th, he went to Shengze and Xiazhe townships in the county to investigate silk.

The Director of the Tobacco and Alcohol Monopoly Bureau Takes Over. The director of the Ministry of Finance's Tobacco and Alcohol Monopoly Taxation Bureau was originally appointed, but this year it was changed to a bidding system. This time, Chen Shaokang, a local resident, won the bid with a price of 50,000 yuan. He has been appointed as the director by the Jiangsu General Bureau. Chen took over on the 15th.

Wuxi 82

The Construction Department Strictly Pursues the Acreage Tax for Road Construction. The Construction Department of Jiangsu Province previously submitted a proposal to the provincial government for discussion and decided that half of the road construction acreage tax from each county should be handed over to the province to cover the construction expenses of national and provincial roads. The provincial government has issued a notice to all counties to comply and the Construction Department has jointly formulated rules with the Finance Department and issued them to all counties to implement the reporting and payment starting in July of this year. The funds are designated to be deposited in the preparatory office of the Jiangsu Provincial Construction Bank. Yesterday, Dong, the director of the Construction Department, telegraphed Chen, the county magistrate of Wuxi, ordering him to supervise the Finance Bureau to submit and report half of the road construction acreage tax collected in July as soon as possible. Any delay that would cause the loss of public funds would be severely punished.

Seventeen Prisoners Granted Amnesty in Xiyi. After receiving the order from the High Court to issue the Amnesty Regulations and the Recidivism Prevention Regulations, the County Court has begun to register the prisoners in the county who are eligible for amnesty and commutation and report them to Wang Simo, the chief prosecutor of the High Court, for review. It has now been determined that the following seventeen prisoners in Wuxi are eligible for the Amnesty Regulations and are approved for release: Zhou Jiaji, Gao Gengen, Song Peigen, Wang Dajin, Zhu Awu, Wang Zhicheng, Chen Runzhi, Sun Xiaoxizi, Bao Genbao, Gu Gengsheng, Su Xiancai, Zheng Asan, Han Baoqing, Tao Jin'er, Fan Baolin, Zhang Fengsheng, and Tang Axi. As for the prisoners who should have their sentences commuted, a list will be compiled and submitted to the court for review.

Rain for Farmland. The county has been suffering from a three-month drought, and both high and low-lying rice fields have been dried up. The farmers are extremely anxious. At around 7 p.m. on the 12th of this month, there was a sudden downpour of about two inches. The countryside received only a slight drizzle, which brought some comfort to the people. The weather has turned autumnal in recent days. Yesterday (the 18th) at around 9 p.m., there was another heavy autumn rain, which lasted until the next morning. The city received about 0.5-0.6 inches of rain. The surrounding areas, such as Dongting, Jiangxi Bridge, Qianqiao, Yangting, Chang'an Bridge, Zhangjing Bridge, Qianzhou, Yuqi, Bei Qifang, and Shitangwan, received about an inch of rain. Although the farmland has not been saturated, it is already felt to be a gift from heaven.

Cocoon Ship and Navigation Ship Robbed Simultaneously. At around 4 a.m. yesterday morning, a small barge carrying eight packages of dried cocoons and eight passengers, owned by Yang A'ba, sailed from Qingyang Town in Cheng County to Wuxi. Unexpectedly, when it passed the vicinity of the Shangshu Temple in Baitangwei, Ni'jiawan, it was suddenly attacked by a pirate ship. Seven pirates jumped out, each wielding firearms, bayonets, and other weapons. They boarded the ship, silenced the passengers, and looted at will. Seven packages of dried cocoons, three dou of white rice belonging to the passengers, thirty-seven yuan in cash, and other scattered items were robbed. After the pirates had plundered their loot and were about to escape, a night navigation ship sailing from Wuxi to Qingyang happened to pass by the area and was robbed simultaneously, losing fifty-four packages of cotton yarn, one roll of Luo sieve, and thirty yuan in cash. After the pirates had fully looted, they returned to their pirate ship, raised their sails, and fled. Lin Rinquan, the owner of the navigation ship, and Yang A'ba, the owner of the barge, seeing the pirate ship fleeing, hired two fishing boats and pursued them closely. They chased them to the vicinity of Hujia Ferry, where it was already dawn and there were pedestrians on the motor road along the bank. Yang and others shouted loudly while continuing their pursuit. Local villagers on the shore called the county government to report the incident. The county dispatched political police officer Wang Wenzhi and others to pursue them by car. They spotted the pirates near Xicun. Seeing the situation was not good, the pirates abandoned their boat and landed, fleeing in the direction of Chang'an Bridge. The original stolen goods were found on the pirate ship, but the cash had been taken away. Wang Wenzhi and others took the pirate ship back to the city to report to the county for handling.

Changzhou 83

County Chamber of Commerce Holds Business Tax Meeting. The Wuyi County Southern Association held a business tax meeting on the 18th. More than thirty representatives from various industries and Zhang Peng, the county magistrate, and Xu Fengtai, the director of the business tax bureau, attended and expressed their opinions. At that time, it was resolved that (1) the business tax bureau would send the declaration forms to the association, which would forward them to the various industries to fill out and return within three days; (2) for stores that are not members of the association, the bureau would send personnel to fill out the forms from the day or order them to fill out and send themselves. In addition, a report was attached from the Wujin 12th Branch of the Shanghai Blood Vengeance Anti-Traitor Corps, advising all industries not to buy enemy goods anymore.

Chengyi Security Corps Captures Bandits in Anqiao. Jiang Jianyin, the deputy commander of the 6th District Security Corps of Cheng County, recently uncovered a ransom ticket for Xie Yuankang from the 8th District and captured many bandits. On the 18th, the deputy commander led his men in Anqiao, a place bordering the old Anxiang district of Wujin, and captured Li Shengtian, an important bandit leader. He was taken to the Public Security Bureau in the city, and a telegram was sent to Cheng County to send police to Changzhou to take him back.

Yangzhou 84

Chief of the Third District Accused of Embezzlement. It has been repeatedly reported in this newspaper that the chiefs of various autonomous districts are being accused of embezzlement. In addition to Zang Liuqi, the chief of the second district, and Guo Zhaoqi, the chief of the seventh district, who are being investigated, Tao Hongru, the chief of the third district, has also been accused by Zhang and others from the district, who have submitted evidence of embezzlement and dereliction of duty to the party and government organs, requesting his removal. Yesterday (the 17th), the County Party Committee sent Tong Nian to investigate. It is said that the allegations are not groundless.

The Perpetrator of the Cen Yingguo Robbery Case Apprehended. The County Public Security Bureau recently received a tip-off that the bandit who robbed Cen Yingguo and shot the victim in the western district was hiding near Dayi. It immediately secretly ordered the investigation team to send detectives. They captured three brothers, Bian Shichang and Kui Shicai, at Gaozhuang, along with sharp weapons. They were taken to the city yesterday, interrogated, and then sent to the Public Security Bureau to be dealt with by the county.

Gaoyou 85

Election of Executive and Supervisory Committee Members Involved in Malpractice. The Fifth County Representative Assembly of this county opened on the 15th of this month. Yesterday, all the important cases were discussed and completed. This morning (the 17th) at 11:00 a.m., the Fourth Executive and Supervisory Committee members were elected. Zhang Mingshun, an instructor from the Provincial Party Department, supervised the election. As a result, Huang Songtao, Zhang Tingjie, and Chen Jiaxiang were elected as executive committee members; Ding Fengnian and Zhang Zhengbang were elected as alternate executive committee members; Wang Tingfan was elected as supervisory committee member; and Zhang Jinshi was elected as alternate supervisory committee member. After the election, Zhang Jinshi, the county representative No. 3, said, "Director Zhang, please pay attention to the fact that this election has been completely manipulated by the old executive and supervisory committee members. The Gaoyou County Party Department and the entire Gaoyou have always been controlled by a small number of party members. They discussed this election in advance, and the election is just a formality." Jinshi will report the details of their malpractice to the Provincial Party Department in a separate article, etc. The closing ceremony was held at 3:00 p.m.

A Disturbance Occurred During the Election in the Tenth District. Gu Jichang, the chief of the tenth district of the county, was previously ordered to handle the election of township chiefs. When the township chiefs of Zhaohe Town, Zhoujin Township, Guoqiao Township, and Xiaji Township were elected at the County No. 2 Elementary School the day before yesterday, Jin Ruijun, the leader of the district regiment, suddenly led his younger brother Ruizhen and armed militiamen to the scene and demanded blank ballots from Chief Gu. Because Gu refused, he was beaten and insulted, and the militiamen were ordered to disperse the public, which aroused public indignation. Currently, Chief Gu and the heads of the various townships, the heads of the farmers' associations, and the public have filed complaints with the Ministry of Interior, the Department of Civil Affairs, the County Government, and other agencies, requesting that the regiment leader be arrested and severely punished.

Nantong 86

Investigating Smuggling of Military Supplies in Various Ports. The Nantong County Government received a letter from Zhu, the head of the Security Regiment stationed in Nantong, stating that according to recent intelligence, heavy boxes have been secretly transported ashore from the seaports of Renting Port and Yao Port in Nantong, and Qinglong Port in Haimen, and secretly sent to the inland. In view of the current disaster situation and the restlessness of the bandits and communists, it is difficult to guarantee that they are not smuggling military supplies in an attempt to launch a riot. In addition to ordering his subordinates to pay attention, he requested the County Magistrate to strictly order the Public Security Bureau to send more officers to the above-mentioned ports to conduct strict inspections to prevent chaos. County Magistrate Zhang ordered the Public Security Bureau's police team and special police team to cooperate with the security regiment to investigate various ports along the river and sea on the 18th.

County Government Investigates Drought Conditions in Various Districts. Since the beginning of summer, there has been little rainfall in Tongyi, and drought has been observed. There are differences in the amount of rainfall in the various districts that have been fortunate enough to receive rain. The county government has already sent investigators.

Huzhou 87

Outbreak of Epidemic Claims Four Lives. In Yuanjiawei, a place in the southern part of the city, the mother-in-law of Ma Sanyuan, a fishmonger, who lived in Digang, recently visited a sick neighbor, contracted the epidemic, and developed the illness after returning home. Within six hours, she and her neighbor died at the same time. Ma Sanyuan's wife, upon hearing the news, went to mourn her mother, also contracted the infection, and the next day hired a young farmer to carry Ma's wife back to Shanghai Huizhi for treatment. The treatment was not enough, and she died soon after. The young farmer also contracted the epidemic and died after returning to Digang.

Discussion of Review Reports

Physical Education Goals Group Passes Five Physical Education Goals 90

Shang Shumei Reports on the Review Results

First, Shang Shumei, the document committee member of the group, made an oral report on the overall review results obtained from previous small group meetings. After the report, the chairman handed it over to the general meeting for discussion. The main points of each review result and the discussion situation are recorded as follows:

The group reviewed the following cases:

Review of Each Case 91

1. Case: Seriously promote the balanced development of all parts of the human body. (Review opinion: Supplement the word "average" within the first item of the draft implementation plan target, that is, to provide sufficient average development opportunities between national physical bodies.)

2. Case: Determine the national physical education policy. (Review opinion) The original case is established. The points raised in it have been mentioned in the draft implementation plan. Regarding the cultivation of national morality in the reasons for the original case and the emphasis on moral cultivation in the methods, it is adopted in the target.

3. Case: School physical education should pay attention to the universal improvement of the health of all students. (Review opinion) The points mentioned in the reasons for the original case have been mentioned in the draft implementation plan. Regarding the methods, it is transferred to the evaluation group for review.

4. Case: Advocate national martial arts to revitalize the inherent national spirit. (Review opinion) The reasons for the original case, such as promoting the national spirit, are adopted in the fourth item of the draft implementation plan target and supplemented as promoting the national spirit and cultivating the national chivalrous and brave spirit. If the original case's methods one and three are transferred to the implementation and promotion group for review, and its second article is changed to the research group for review.

5. Case: Please promote the health and beauty of men. (Review opinion) Supplement the original case, and add the nine characters [and cultivate the concept of healthy beauty] under the first item of the draft implementation plan target. Note: The addition of the nine characters was cancelled by the general meeting on the morning of the 17th.

6. Case: Determine the policy of promoting national physical education. (Review opinion) The original case raised two main points. One [hard work and endurance] is supplemented into the fourth item of the draft implementation plan target, that is, [:::: cultivate the national chivalrous, brave, hard-working and enduring spirit]. The second point raised has been included in the second item of the draft implementation plan and will no longer be discussed.

According to the above review results, the goal of supplementing the draft national physical education implementation plan, the full text is as left:

(1) Provide the people with ample opportunities for the average development of their bodies.

(2) Train the people to use their bodies randomly to adapt to their environment.

(3) Cultivate the spirit of cooperation and unity among the people.

(4) Promote the national spirit and cultivate the spirit of chivalry, bravery, hard work, and endurance among the people.

(5) Cultivate the people's habit of using sports and games for entertainment.

Review Results 92

According to the review results, the goal of supplementing the draft national physical education implementation plan is revised as follows:

(1) Provide the people with ample and average opportunities for the development of their bodies.

(2) Train the people to use their bodies randomly to adapt to their environment.

(3) Cultivate the spirit of cooperation and unity among the people.

(4) Promote the national spirit and cultivate the spirit of chivalry, bravery, hard work, and endurance among the people.

(5) Cultivate the people's habit of using sports and games for entertainment

Discussion Results

The five goals are passed according to the review results. Yuan Dunli proposed that the review opinions be passed and submitted to the program organizing committee for organization. Hao Gengsheng seconded, and it was passed without objection.

Administrative Organization Group 93

Yuan Dunli Reports on the Review Results

First, Yuan Dunli, the chairman of the group, made an oral report on the review results obtained from previous small group meetings (the same as the written report, omitted). After the report, the chairman handed it over to the general meeting for discussion. The main points of each review result and the discussion situation are recorded as follows:

There are many proposals in this group. The results of the review and merger are as follows. Among them, (1), (2), (3), and (4) belong to the administrative aspects, (5) and (6) belong to the financial aspects, and (7), (8), and (9) belong to the meeting organization aspects.

(1) Educational administrative organs at all levels should set up physical education supervisors. The Ministry of Education, departments and bureaus should quickly set up physical education supervisors and instructors to supervise the local and school physical education facilities, plans, and improvements. Based on facts, make important suggestions.

(2) The Ministry of Education, departments, and bureaus should set up physical education committees and add physical education sections, departments, groups, and specialize in the design and administrative matters of school and social physical education in their respective jurisdictions under the Social Education Division. (3) [Proposed National Physical Education Administrative System Case] A central physical education association should be set up in the central government, and physical education associations at all levels should be set up separately in provinces, cities, counties, districts, and villages. Each physical education association should have general affairs, organization, training, publicity, translation, statistics, and other departments, as well as education museums, central or first-class municipal sports fields, research institutes, etc. Review opinions are submitted to the general meeting for reference.

(4) National martial arts departments should be set up in sports fields in various provinces, cities, and counties to promote them.

(5) In addition to the physical education fees paid by students, physical education funds at all levels of schools should be determined in the budget and stipulate that the number should account for at least 5% of the total school expenses (but the principle is that student physical education fees should not be collected; some also advocate that student fees should not be excluded from the 5%).

(6) [Proposed to re-levy luxury and hobby taxes to fill the physical education and martial arts fund case] Review opinions are submitted to the general meeting for reference.

(7) The National Games are held every two years, and are designated by the Ministry of Education and the National Physical Education Commission to be held in various provinces in rotation.

Sports meetings are held once a year in each province, city, and county. The methods are determined by the physical education committees of the educational departments and bureaus of each province, city, and county.

A national martial arts movement should be added to sports meetings in various provinces, cities, and counties. Sports meetings are held once a year in schools at all levels.

(8) Athletes participating in various sports meetings at all levels must first undergo academic, moral, age, physical, and amateur qualification reviews. The standards and methods are researched and determined by the Physical Education Commission of the Ministry of Education.

(9) The case of amending the amateur sports rules, together with other rules, is submitted to the Competition Sports Regulations Committee of the Ministry of Education for research and revision.

Discussion Results Passed: Ministry of Education to Establish a Physical Education Supervisor's Office, Education Bureau to Establish a Physical Education Guidance Office 94

(I) Proposal for Establishing Physical Education Supervisors in Educational Administrative Organs at All Levels

Liu Shenzhan explained the necessity of having an independent physical education administrative organization and funding.

Yuan Dunli argued that physical education is part of education, and physical education administration cannot be independent.

Zhou Gan and Shao Rugan agreed with Yuan's view. Shao said that physical education administration is different from the National Martial Arts Institute, which is a research institution, and cannot be independent.

Wu Bangwei and Ma Yuehan said that as long as practical measures can be implemented, independence or non-independence is irrelevant.

Chairman Chu, representing Minister Zhu, explained that the Ministry of Education agreed to the establishment of physical education supervisors.

Wang Zhengting said that since the government is paying attention to promoting physical education, its effectiveness will be greater than that of the people's promotion, and advocated passing the proposal according to the review opinions.

Chen Shizhen argued that the Ministry of Education's office could specifically establish a physical education supervisor's office, but independent establishment in each county seems impossible.

Yuan Dunli and others agreed with Chen Shizhen's opinion.

Shao Rugan proposed amending the review proposal to "[Ministry of Education office to quickly establish a physical education supervisor, education bureau to establish inspectors and instructors]." After Xu Zhiyi's amendment, "[inspectors and instructors]" was changed to "[instructors]". The proposer accepted the amendment. Wu Yunrui, Yuan Dunli, Chen Shizhen, and others seconded the proposal. The proposal was established. The chairman put it to a vote, and the majority approved, resolving that the Ministry of Education office quickly establish a physical education supervisor and the education bureau quickly establish physical education instructors to guide the facilities, plans, and improvements of local and school physical education in their jurisdictions, and to make essential suggestions based on facts.

Passed: Physical Education Administration to Be Handled by Educational Organs at All Levels 95

(II) Educational administrative organs at all levels should each establish a physical education committee and add physical education sections, divisions, and teams under the Social Education Department, divisions, and bureaus. Chairman Chu said that this proposal and the third proposal have different opinions on the organization of physical education administration and should first discuss whether the organization of physical education administration should be independent.

Xu Zhiyi and others argued that physical education administration should fall within the scope of education administration. After discussion, the majority agreed with Xu's argument.

The chairman put it to a vote and passed, resolving that physical education administration be handled by educational administrative organs at all levels.

Passed: Educational Administrative Organs at All Levels Should Establish Physical Education Committees and Separate Physical Education Sections 96

(III) Physical Education Administration Should Be Handled by Educational Administrative Organs at All Levels

I. Chairman Chu announced that this review proposal would be put to discussion.

II. Gu Shusen and Xu Zhiyi argued that physical education is not only related to social education but also to the higher education and general education divisions within the Ministry of Education. The phrase "[under the Social Education Department divisions and bureaus]" in this proposal should be deleted.

III. Chen Shizhen said that the physical education committee seems to have already stipulated administrative functions. Whether to set up another section should be discussed.

IV. Yuan Dunli argued that the physical education committee should be discussed first as to whether it should be established.

V. The chairman put to a vote whether educational administrative organs at all levels should establish physical education committees. All agreed and passed, resolving that educational administrative organs at all levels should establish physical education committees.

VI. Chairman Chu put to discussion whether to establish a section outside the physical education committee.

VII. Yuan Dunli argued that the resolutions of the committee should be approved by the Minister of Education and separately handed over to the standing committee members, physical education supervisors, and the responsible departments to implement, and there is no need to set up a special physical education section.

VIII. Gu Shusen argued that the committee should only be responsible for design and not兼管administrative duties. Administrative duties should be handled by a section.

1. Hao Gengsheng, Chen Jianai, Shao Rugan, Liu Shenzhan, Sun Mingxiu, Du Longyuan, Jin Zhaojun, and Su Jingyou successively expressed their opinions, either advocating for or against the establishment of a section. Shao Rugan, who advocated for the establishment of a section, said that since there is a design committee to guide and supervisors, there should also be a section established for the implementation aspect. Du Longyuan, who did not advocate for the establishment of a section, said that there are already standing committee members in the committee who can兼管 administrative duties. Physical education administration in the Ministry of Education should belong to various departments and should not be established as a section to handle it.

X. Chairman Chu put to a vote whether to "[establish a physical education section outside the physical education committee]". Forty-five people voted in favor of establishing a section, and forty-four people voted against establishing a section. The resolution was passed with those who voted in favor of establishing a section. However, since the difference in votes was very small, the opinions of those who did not agree should also be recorded and submitted to the Ministry of Education for reference.

(III) National Physical Education Administrative System Proposal

This proposal has already been voted on simultaneously with the second proposal. Since the second proposal was established, this proposal should not be established.

Provinces Take Turns Hosting

(III) The proposal to hold the National Games every two years and take turns in the provinces. Wang Zhengting agreed. The review proposal of every two years saves students' time. Passed: Each City and County to Hold Sports Meet Once Every Year 102

(V) Proposal for each province, city, and county to hold a sports meet every year, and martial arts should be added during the event. 1. Regarding the addition of martial arts, there was no second, and it was passed. 2. Yang Zhaoshi proposed that the period for holding sports meets every year should be stipulated during the holidays, such as winter vacation, summer vacation, spring vacation, and Double Ten Festival. 3. Wang Zhengting said that holding sports meets during winter and summer vacations is considered inappropriate in all countries. The spring vacation and Double Ten Festival are very short and also inappropriate, so the period cannot be specified. Yang's proposal was not established. 4. Du Longyuan said that holding sports meets once a year takes too much time. If the number of meetings is too many, students' study time will inevitably be reduced and should be noted. 5. However, each city should still hold it once every year. The original proposer expressed acceptance. The amendment was established. 7. Jin Zhaojun advocated maintaining the original proposal. 8. The chairman put the amendment to a vote, with twenty-two people in favor, a small minority rejecting it. 9. The chairman put the review proposal that each province, city, and county hold a sports meet every year to a vote, and it passed.

III. The members must be physical education experts and those who have researched martial arts, and should be appointed by the Ministry of Education.

Passed: Martial Arts Guidance Should Be Established in Sports Venues in Provinces, Cities, and Counties 108

(IV) Proposal for each province, city, and county sports field to establish a martial arts department to promote it. 1. The plan has been determined to first establish a training center, wanting to integrate physical education and martial arts. Martial artists should be physicalized, and physical educators should be martialized.

10. Zhang Zhijiang said that martial arts has a history and is very important, and instructors must be set up.

XI. The chairman put the review to a vote, and sixty-five votes passed by a majority. The method is as follows:

Martial arts should be established in the sports fields of each province, city, and county. Those areas where martial arts halls have not yet been established should be implemented as soon as possible and should hire specialized martial arts talents to serve as instructors to broaden the training.

The Opinion of the Educational Circles in Ping is That the Conference Should Not Be Superstitious About European and American Sports 119

Nanjing, 19th Telegram: The conference received a telegram from 124 people including Yu Xiao and Li Zheng from the educational circles in Ping, which read: We hope that you will not be too superstitious about European, American, and Japanese imported sports methods, but will selectively adopt the good martial arts inherent in our country. The various sports theories advocated by Chairman Chu in recent years, such as advocating that sports should be able to benefit everyone, regardless of gender or age, and should regard exercise as equal to diet, and extremely oppose people who are sports experts and the name of sports experts, and such as saying that the purpose of exercise is only to strengthen the body, so the method of exercise should not take competition and competition, and such as saying that physical education methods must meet the three "no" principles: no money, no effort, and no time, it is easy to popularize and effective. The colleagues firmly believe that these points are the correct theories for those who talk about physical education today and the path and direction that the educational circles in our country must take. We sincerely hope that you will pay attention to this. Taijiquan especially meets the above-mentioned sports principles, and we sincerely hope that it can be decided by your conference to submit it to the Ministry of Education to order all primary and secondary schools in the country to list it as a compulsory physical education course.

8. Situation of athletes taking the oath at the opening ceremony

Overview of Sports in Various Places Zhejiang 120

On April 1, the 19th year of the Republic of China, the National Games was held in Hangzhou. After the closing ceremony, all the venues were accepted and managed by the Zhejiang Provincial Department of Education, which was the origin of the Zhejiang Provincial Stadium. Later, through Mr. Chen Baiqing's hard work, Zhejiang sports circles began to see a glimmer of dawn, with perfect organization and well-equipped facilities. Regarding the organization of sports meets at all levels, it is divided into four types: provincial, regional, county/city, and school, with the school as the basis and the province as the destination. The county/city sports meet includes primary and secondary school students and amateurs, and is held in groups. The regional is held by gathering schools above the secondary level. The expenses are borne by the schools concerned or the educational authorities of each department. As for the treatment of physical education teachers in middle schools, it is very good, between one and a half yuan and one yuan per hour, and all seek to meet the standards. Now, the Hangzhou Stadium is planning to build a swimming pool to increase public interest, which is jointly run by the province and the city. The funding has been secured and has already begun construction. Swimming is the most suitable exercise, which is of great benefit to public health. Chinese people often ignore it. In most large cities, there is not even one, which is what our sports community cannot compare with other countries. This is one of them. This autumn, the third Zhejiang Provincial Games will be held in Hangzhou. It is said that there will be many new items and new performance styles. At that time, there will be a grand occasion.

The telegram reads as follows: To Mr. Wu Yan of the Ministry of Education, transfer to Mr. Zhu Jingnong: Brother Lao is ill and unable to fulfill his responsibilities. It is a joy for both public and private affairs to have you succeed me. Hunan is now peaceful, and Mr. Yun is managing affairs well. Educational funds are in place, and there are no other difficulties. Please come immediately so that I can relinquish my responsibilities and comfort the many scholars. Respectfully, Cao Dianqiu.

Local News

Jianghai Customs Announces Implementation of Consular Visa for Invoices 128

The US, Italy, Spain, Finland and Czechoslovakia are Implementing This System

China to Implement it From September 1

Regarding the issue of all countries requiring a Chinese consular visa for goods shipped to China, the Jianghai Customs Superintendent and the Jianghai Customs Commissioner have officially received an order from the Customs Administration of the Ministry of Finance to implement this system starting from September 1. The Customs Superintendent and the Customs Commissioner have jointly issued a proclamation. The details are as follows:

Joint Proclamation by the Jianghai Customs Superintendent and the Customs Commissioner: Regarding the matter of joint proclamation, we have received an order from the Customs Administration of the Ministry of Finance to issue regulations for the issuance of consular visas for invoices by the consulates of the Republic of China abroad, instructing us to comply with and implement them. Therefore, the said regulations are recorded below. All goods shipped from overseas to China from September 1, 1932, must comply with the provisions of these regulations. The date of shipment of these goods to China shall be based on the date of issuance of the bill of lading related to the goods. This consular visa for the invoice is not intended to replace the original invoice issued by the ordinary merchant. In addition to complying with the regulations to present the consular visa for verification, merchants shall still present the original invoice issued by the merchant to the Customs for verification. Furthermore, the Customs shall not be bound by the prices and other items listed in the consular visa when determining the tax amount. Merchants are hereby notified. Special proclamation. August 18, 1932, Superintendent Tang Hai'an, Acting Customs Commissioner Kedad.

Full Text of the Regulations: Regulations for the Issuance of Consular Visas for Invoices by the Consulates of the Republic of China Abroad. Article 1: From the date of implementation of these regulations, all goods shipped from overseas to China with a value of more than 200 yuan in national currency, except for postal packages and goods exempt from customs duties, must be accompanied by a consular visa for the invoice issued by the Chinese consulate located at or near the place of export. Article 2: The consular visa for the invoice mentioned in the preceding article can be obtained from the nearest consulate of the Republic of China. The merchant must fill in each item clearly and have it signed by the responsible person, and submit it to the Chinese consulate located at or near the place of export for visa. Article 3: The consul shall verify the accuracy of each item filled in the price before issuing a visa. If it is deemed necessary to verify documents or other documents, the merchant shall comply immediately. Article 4: Each set of consular visa for the invoice shall be three copies: one original, which is white; and two copies, which are yellow. The original copy shall be handed over to the merchant by the consulate issuing the consular visa for the invoice and forwarded to the consignee for submission to the Customs for verification. The remaining two copies shall be kept by the consulate, and one copy shall be sent to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs on a monthly basis. Article 5: A handling fee of five gold units of the Customs shall be charged for each consular visa for the invoice and collected at the time of issuance. Article 6: The consular visa fees collected by the consul shall be remitted to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs on a monthly basis along with the copies of the consular visa for the invoice. Article 7: Goods sold to two importing merchants, or loaded on two merchant ships, or imported into two ports, shall not be reported on the same invoice. Article 8: After the goods arrive at the destination, the consignee shall submit the original of the invoice to the Customs for verification at the time of customs declaration. Article 9: For imported goods without a consular visa for the invoice, the consignee shall pay three times the prescribed visa fee as a fine, which shall be used by the Customs to reissue the visa for the invoice before the goods can be released. (A) For goods shipped from overseas on or after September 1, 1932, and reported to the Customs between November and December of the same year without a consular visa for the invoice, the consignee shall pay a visa fee of five gold units of the Customs to the Customs for reissuing the visa for the invoice. (B) For goods shipped from overseas on or after September 1, 1932, and reported to the Customs between November and December of the same year without a consular visa for the invoice, the consignee shall pay twice the above-mentioned visa fee, totaling ten gold units of the Customs, to the Customs for reissuing the visa for the invoice. (C) For goods shipped from overseas on or after January 1, 1932, and reported to the Customs on or after January 1, 1933, without a consular visa for the invoice, the consignee shall pay a fine of fifteen gold units of the Customs to the Customs for reissuing the visa for the invoice, as stipulated in this article of these regulations. (Note:)

The above three items [A], [B], and [C] listed [reporting to Customs for sampling] shall be interpreted as [reporting import] and [reporting storage at the Customs warehouse], and do not refer to reporting transshipment. The date of transshipment of these goods at domestic ports is not relevant to these regulations. Article 10: At the end of each month, the Customs shall list all the consular visas for the invoice collected, together with the amount of fines, and report them to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, and remit the visas and fines to the Customs Administration of the Ministry of Finance. Article 11: The gold unit of the Customs shall be converted by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs according to the exchange rates of the currencies of various countries announced by the Customs, and the consulates shall be ordered to collect fees accordingly. Article 12: The consular visas for the invoice shall be printed and stamped by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and issued to the consulates and the Customs for use. Article 13: Matters not covered by these regulations may be submitted for amendment at any time. Article 14: These regulations shall come into force on September 1, 1932.

Methods of various countries: After the government announced the implementation of the consular visa for goods system, it was heard that the Japanese Consul had raised objections. A reporter from the Xinsheng News Agency specially went to the consulates of various countries in this port to investigate the implementation methods and fee amounts of this system in various countries. The results obtained are as follows: (A) The countries that adopt the consular visa system are: (1) Spain: For goods imported to China, a visa fee of 12 Spanish national currency units, equivalent to 7 Chinese currency units, is charged per piece. (2) Finland: The current method is to charge US$4.50 per sheet. (3) Italy: Each sheet is charged 10 US gold lire, equivalent to 9.10 Chinese currency units. (4) Czechoslovakia: Each sheet is charged 5/1000 of the price listed on the invoice. (5) The United States: US$2.50 per sheet. (B) The countries that do not adopt the consular visa system are: (1) Germany, (2) Belgium, (3) Denmark, (4) The United Kingdom, (5) Sweden, (6) Switzerland, (7) Holland, (8) Norway.

Japanese Businesses Firmly Oppose Implementation of Foreign Consular-Issued Goods Certificates 129

Emergency Meeting to be Held at 1 PM Tomorrow According to Shishi News, after the Customs Superintendent Tang Haian and Customs Commissioner Ketade jointly issued a proclamation yesterday, stipulating that the method of foreign consuls issuing goods certificates will be implemented starting from the first of next month, Japanese commercial groups in this port have scheduled an emergency meeting at 1 PM tomorrow at the Residents' Group in Peng Road to discuss countermeasures. At the same time, they are also conducting liaison with merchants from various countries in Shanghai to confront us collectively. Their letter to fellow friendly foreign merchants has also been drafted and will be issued after textual revisions at tomorrow's emergency meeting. The various news items are recorded separately below.

Emergency Meeting to be Held The holding of this emergency meeting by Japanese businesses is being coordinated and convened by the merchant associations of various roads and has been scheduled for 1 PM tomorrow in the conference room of the Residents' Group on Peng Road. The main agenda item is to oppose the method of foreign consuls issuing goods certificates announced yesterday by our Customs authorities. In addition to the merchant associations of various roads deciding to request their government to promptly lodge a protest with our foreign affairs authorities, they will also widely solicit the opinions of Japanese businesses for reference. As for other matters to be discussed, there are many important issues, such as [how to respond if the Shanghai Municipal Government refuses to accept the protest lodged by Consul-General Murai regarding the activities of the "Blood Soul Assassination Group," etc.] and [how to remedy the increasingly dire situation of the Sino-Japanese trade.]

Conducting Liaison with Foreign Businesses In terms of trade with China, Great Britain, the United States, Japan, and Germany are all in a superior position. Japanese businesses, recognizing that merchants from various countries in Shanghai have not shown any opposition after our side announced the method of foreign consuls issuing goods certificates, believe that it will be difficult to achieve results if they hold dissenting opinions alone. Therefore, Japanese commercial groups in Shanghai have been conducting liaison with merchants from various countries for days, hoping to conspire against us collectively, and are very active. However, the results of the liaison in recent days show that merchants from various countries are mostly taking a wait-and-see attitude and are unwilling to cooperate with Japanese businesses to undermine the friendship between the two sides in international trade. However, Japanese businesses are still not at all aware of this and yesterday still sent out many representatives to various foreign commercial organizations in Shanghai to carry out their wooing tactics in order to achieve their goal of uniting and conspiring against us.

Letter to Fellow Friendly Foreign Merchants In addition to dispatching representatives to conduct liaison with various foreign businesses, Japanese businesses in Shanghai are also issuing a letter to fellow friendly foreign merchants. The full text was drafted yesterday, totaling thousands of words, doing their utmost to sow discord. However, the full text still needs to be textually revised at tomorrow's emergency meeting before it can be officially released. However, according to the reporter's inquiry, the content of the full text can be roughly divided into: (1) After the method of foreign consuls issuing goods certificates is implemented, trade with China by various countries will be severely hit. (2) The Chinese government, in order to secretly carry out a plan to exclude foreign goods, has specifically implemented the method of foreign consuls issuing goods certificates. (3) If fellow merchants from friendly countries who are related to trade with China do not oppose the method of foreign consuls issuing goods certificates implemented by the Chinese government this time, it is tantamount to cutting off their own lifeline in trade with China. These are their absurd arguments used as reasons for opposing it.

Reasons for Japanese Businesses' Opposition Since the "September 18th Incident" last year, Japan's foreign trade has plummeted due to the impact of our country's boycott of Japanese goods. In addition, the activities of the "Blood Soul Assassination Group" and the circular issued by the municipal chamber of commerce to various industries refusing to import Japanese raw materials have dealt a fatal blow to Japanese businesses. Although Japanese businesses have tried their best to reduce the cost of various goods, their business has not improved at all. At a time when they are extremely anxious about trade with China, our country has formulated 14 articles on the method of foreign consuls issuing goods certificates, scheduled for implementation, which will result in Japanese businesses having to bear an additional burden of paying eight yuan for the certificate fee for every hundred yuan when shipping goods to China. This will inevitably increase the cost of various goods. At a time when trade with China is becoming increasingly dire, losses will become even greater. Therefore, Japanese businesses will definitely firmly oppose the method of foreign consuls issuing goods certificates formulated by the Ministry of Finance announced by our Customs yesterday.

Japanese Military Crossing the Border into the Chinese Concession is of a Temporary Nature 130

Yu Hongjun Refutes the Japanese Consul's Absurd Claim

Regarding the Japanese military crossing the border to demonstrate, the Municipal Government has lodged a serious protest, which has been repeatedly reported in the newspapers. However, with respect to the claim made by the Japanese Deputy Consul yesterday that Japanese soldiers passed through Zhongshan Road due to the handover of defense, which was based on an understanding, Yu Hongjun, Secretary-General of the Municipal Government, made a statement yesterday stating that when the Japanese military withdrew from Zhabei on May 23, 25 Japanese soldiers each remained at the Toyota Yarn Factory and the Tongwen Academy. At that time, the Japanese handover committee negotiated with our receiving committee that during the period when the Japanese soldiers were temporarily stationed at the Toyota Yarn Factory and the Tongwen Academy, the Japanese military could temporarily pass through Zhongshan Road for the purpose of defense handover and supplying food. Later, the Japanese representative of the Joint Committee reported to the chairman of the committee, who informed our representative. Our representative, upon receiving the report, considered that the Japanese military was withdrawing in stages, and the Japanese soldiers at the Toyota Yarn Factory and the Tongwen Academy had not yet been withdrawn, so this understanding was still needed in reality. Therefore, he did not

Express opposition, but declared to the Joint Committee that this approach should cease once Japan, in accordance with the agreement, withdraws its troops stationed at the Toyota Yarn Factory and the Tongwen Academy. Therefore, the understanding at that time was a temporary measure. Now, the Japanese military at the Tongwen Academy has already withdrawn, and there is no reason for the Japanese military to remain at the Toyota Yarn Factory. Our representative has repeatedly engaged in stern negotiations, and the excuse of the Japanese Deputy Consul is actually a forced interpretation.

Unscrupulous Merchants Mail Inferior Piece Goods to Sichuan and Hunan 131

Secretly re-packaged inferior piece goods have recently been imported continuously. When loaded onto ships to Shanghai, many of them have already had their lot numbers changed, falsely claiming to be domestic goods and mixing into the market. The Customs Inspection Team has already discovered a batch. Recently, unscrupulous merchants transporting and selling inferior goods upstream of the Yangtze River have come up with an absurd idea. They have secretly hired a large number of workers in a certain foreign warehouse in Hongkou to unpack the renamed inferior goods and repack them into small packages. This work has been going on for many days, in preparation for sneaking them out of the country to various ports in Sichuan and Hunan.

Unscrupulous merchants shipping inferior goods to the upper reaches of the Yangtze River send eight or nine out of ten shipments to Chongqing, Wanxian, Chengdu in Sichuan, and various ports in Hunan Province. Because they believe it is not easy to ship by ship, they have changed their approach. After packing them into small packages, they send them from a certain dock warehouse in Hongkou to the post office as parcel mail to avoid inspection. In this one sentence, six or seven hundred pieces have already been sent out. Now, the unscrupulous merchants have hired more workers to rush to pack and seal the packages day and night and send them in batches.

Shipping is in Sharp Decline Shanghai-Chuan River merchant ships rely entirely on the transportation of piece goods. Recently, after unscrupulous merchants re-branded inferior goods and mailed them through the post office, the export business of Chongqing-bound river ships has been greatly affected. Freight has sharply declined. Taikoo, Jardine, and other upper Yangtze River ships have recently announced a sharp drop in the water freight rates for piece goods from Shanghai to Chongqing in order to attract cargo, reducing the rate from ten taels to eight taels per piece.

Agreement on the Return of the Dutch Boxer Indemnity Largely Reached 134

The outstanding amount is still over 500,000 taels of Customs Silver

It is proposed to use it to purchase machinery and materials from the Netherlands

Central News Agency reports that the Ministry of Foreign Affairs has held several consultations with Dutch Minister to China Oudendijk on the issue of the return of the Dutch Boxer Indemnity and has reached a substantial result. However, due to the Dutch Minister's return to his country, it was temporarily suspended. After the new Dutch Minister, de Péric, arrived in China, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs immediately continued the process and has largely reached an agreement, which can be signed soon.

The total amount of the Dutch Boxer Indemnity The total amount of the Dutch Boxer Indemnity that China should pay is 2,474,912.77 Dutch guilders, equivalent to 1,378,013.82 taels of Customs Silver. It was stipulated at the time that it would be paid off in 29 years from 1912 to 1940. From 1912 to 1914, 62,114.64 Dutch guilders should be repaid each year; in 1915, 72,677.60 Dutch guilders should be repaid; from 1916 to 1931, 76,424.9 Dutch guilders should be repaid each year; from 1932 to 1940, 110,343.65 Dutch guilders should be repaid each year. By the end of 1931, the amount that had been repaid totaled 1,481,819.92 Dutch guilders, equivalent to 825,066.78 taels of our country's

Customs Silver. The amount that had not been repaid was 9,930,922.85 Dutch guilders, equivalent to our country's

Customs Silver 552,947.04 taels.

A resolution can be reached soon According to personnel from the Dutch Consulate in this port, Dutch Minister de Péric has agreed with the Chinese foreign affairs authorities in Nanjing on the details regarding the return of the Dutch Boxer Indemnity. The Shanghai Consulate has not learned of the details. However, according to the reporter's inquiry, it is heard that China and the Netherlands have decided to use the funds to purchase machinery and timber from the Netherlands after the Dutch Boxer Indemnity is returned. Once these conditions are agreed upon, it can be signed.
