The Municipal Chamber of Commerce Executive and Supervisory Committee Resolves to Thoroughly Investigate Zhang Rongchu According to the Law 142

Counterfeiting the Trademark of the Printing and Dyeing Company

Conspiring to Obtain Illegal Profits

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce convened an emergency meeting of the Executive and Supervisory Committee yesterday regarding the Shanghai Printing and Dyeing Company case. The Executive and Supervisory Committee members Bei Songsun, Wang Yansong, Du Yuesheng, Lao Jingxiu, Fang Jiaobo, Wen Lanting, Ma Jiliang, Zheng Zenan, Lu Wenshao, Jiang Zhigang, Pan Xusheng, Luo Qinghua, Ma Shaoquan, Ye Jiaxing, and others attended. As Chairman Wang Xiaolai went to Sanmen Bay for inspection, Wang Yansong was elected as the temporary chairman, and Secretary Yan Esheng took the minutes. The Commerce Section of the Secretariat reported on the handling and investigation of the Shanghai Printing and Dyeing Company case. After careful discussion, the attendees unanimously resolved as follows: (1) The company's board of directors is responsible for thoroughly investigating Zhang Rongchu, who is highly suspected in this case, and all accomplices according to the law. (2) The goods detained in Xiangtan must be verified by the Chamber of Commerce before being processed. (3) The company should report a detailed list of incoming and outgoing goods to the Chamber of Commerce at any time for investigation.

The Secretariat reported on the Shanghai Printing and Dyeing Company case. The Chamber of Commerce received a letter from the company on the 28th of this month, stating that they had received letters from cloth merchants in Xiangtan, Hunan, stating that the "San Xingqi Zhigong Biji" and other goods purchased from the company and transported to Xiangtan were detained by the Xiangtan Anti-Japanese Association. They requested a prompt letter of proof and the immediate return of the detained goods. The Chamber of Commerce pointed out that the company was only engaged in printing and dyeing, not spinning and weaving. The key issue was the source of the cloth. When the Chamber of Commerce issued a certificate in the past, it sent personnel to investigate. The company's cloth坯 was contracted from Shenxin Textile Factory all year round, but Shenxin Factory only wove ordinary cloth疋头, not Zhigong or Biji. Moreover, according to the investigation at the time, the factory's annual output was only 60,000疋. In addition, it was claimed that Jianhua Shenji Weaving Factory also had transactions with the company. However, Jianhua was located on Tiantong'an Road in Zhabei and had been shut down since the Shanghai Incident, with no goods to supply. Therefore, external suspicions about the company had been heard from time to time recently. In the spirit of seeking truth from facts, the Chamber of Commerce should ask the company to provide detailed information on the monthly demand for cloth坯 and which cloth factories supplied it, so as to re-verify and certify. After the letter was sent, the company replied on the 29th, stating that the company's cloth坯 was purchased from major yarn factories and foreign firms such as Tianxiang, Jardine Matheson, and Carlowitz. The previous contract with Shenxin did not include Zhigong Biji. The 60,000疋 mentioned were completely printed plain cloth坯, but each疋 was 120 yards long, which was four times the 30 yards of cloth processed and sold by the company. Currently, the company had ordered 42,000疋 of the same cloth坯 from Tianxiang, all 120 yards long. Although less than half had been released due to the cloth surface, the number of 30-yard pieces was also very large. In addition, Jianhua Cloth Factory had a contract with the company to purchase cloth坯, including three types: Zhigong, Biji, and twill. Before the war, it had delivered 72,000疋 of Zhigong (30 yards) and 54,000疋 of Biji (30 yards). At that time, it was approaching the end of the year, and the market was declining, so the company stacked the cloth坯 completely after processing. It only started to move slightly this spring. The cost of Zhigong呢 shipped to Xiangtan was about 9 taels, but it was now selling for only 6 taels and 7 qian 5 fen. They felt heartbroken to sell at a loss, but unexpectedly, it was still seized by the Anti-Japanese Association in Xiangtan. They requested an immediate telegram to release the goods and to inform the Xiangtan Chamber of Commerce for certification. The letter also pointed out that the Municipal Chamber of Commerce could not protect industry, accusing them of convicting people based on suspicion. After receiving the letter, the Chamber of Commerce still believed that it could not be easily certified without a thorough investigation. The Chamber of Commerce immediately instructed the Commerce Section to investigate secretly. On August 4, the Chamber of Commerce received another letter from the company, attaching a copy of the date of purchase, sales, product name, and quantity list, requesting verification and certification. It was approved and transferred to the Commerce Section for joint investigation.

Standing Committee: Due to the importance of the matter, the Chamber of Commerce submitted it to the seventh meeting of the Standing Committee on the 11th of this month. Those present that day included Wang Xiaolai, Wang Yansong, Bei Songsun, Lu Wenshao, four standing committee members, Chen Zheqing, Luo Qinghua, two directors, and Yan Esheng, the secretary. Chairman Wang Xiaolai presided over the meeting. After discussion, it was decided that the case would be handed over to the Commerce Section for a thorough investigation to clarify the truth. At the eighth Standing Committee meeting on the 18th, the Commerce Section had completed its investigation of the case and reported the investigation results in detail. Those present that day included Wang Xiaolai, Wang Yansong, Bei Songsun, Yu Zuoting, Lu Wenshao, five standing committee members, Chen Wuqing, Luo Qinghua, two directors, and Yan Esheng, the secretary. After discussion, three opinions were formulated and a joint meeting of the Executive and Supervisory Committee was convened today to discuss them.

Zhou Yanqing Case: Regarding the Shanghai Printing and Dyeing Company's own report that its employee Zhou Yanqing had set up an organization to mix Japanese goods with the company's products, all letters are as follows: (1) The Printing and Dyeing Company sent a letter to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce on August 8, stating: "Respectfully, due to frequent misunderstandings about our factory's products in foreign locations, we sincerely request your association to send personnel to investigate and provide re-certification to facilitate the circulation of national goods. We have dared to stomach the violation and are waiting for instructions. However, the outside world is unaware and rumors are rampant. It is even rumored that our company is repackaging and selling enemy goods under false pretenses. Such misinterpretations will inevitably increase your association's doubts. We will truthfully detail the facts of the rumors below. Previously, our company's canvasser, Zhou Yanqing, set up an organization on Pingliang Road in July to transform enemy goods into our company's trademarks and sell them in the market. Fortunately, the Yulin Road Police Station cracked down on the transformation organization and immediately notified our company to investigate. Our company sent personnel to the police station and found that the seized trademarks were 80% our company's. Therefore, our company filed a case for arrest. Later, because Zhou Yanqing's elderly father, over seventy years old, led his daughter-in-law and his grandchildren to beg our company bitterly, our company temporarily proposed at the 63rd emergency meeting of the board of directors whether the case should be pursued. After the board of directors decided to consider their poverty and pity them, they did not pursue the matter and dismissed the employee, and he wrote a letter of repentance. They gave up the right to appeal. However, the outside world does not know the truth and misinterprets this matter, fearing that it will confuse the wise. We have submitted the circumstances and a photograph of the original repentant for your review. Sincerely, Shanghai Printing and Dyeing Co., Ltd." (2) Attached is a video of Zhou Yanqing's letter of repentance: "Letter of repentance from Zhou Yanqing. I know that I was blinded by profit and dared to set up an organization on Pingliang Road to counterfeit your company's trademarks and transform Japanese goods to pass off as your company's products. I was investigated and arrested by the Yulin Road Police Station. Yanqing's illegal behavior is punishable, but due to a momentary mistake, I vow not to engage in trademark infringement again in the future. I beg your company to be extra merciful, considering my first offense, and give me a chance to reform. I will repay you with gratitude. Fearing that my words are unfounded, I am writing this letter of repentance for the record. Respectfully, Shanghai Printing and Dyeing Company, July 28, 1932, letter of repentance Zhou Yanqing (signed)." (3) The Printing and Dyeing Company's Board of Directors sent a letter to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce on August 16, stating: "Respectfully, recently, there have been many criticisms of our company's products. Your association has sent personnel to thoroughly investigate the truth and has shown commendable patriotism and support for commerce. We believe that there is a reason for rumors. Therefore, on August 8, we detailed the case of our runner, Zhou Yanqing, fraudulently selling British company and our company's trademarks outside, which was discovered by the police station. We immediately convened the 63rd board of directors meeting and decided to dismiss him. Because of his poverty, we did not pursue the matter and only asked Zhou Yanqing to write a letter of repentance. However, the outside world does not understand the content, and rumors continue to circulate. On August 12, we convened an emergency board of directors meeting, and all members agreed that the employee's fraud of using the company's trademark for personal gain and corruption was a serious matter, and only dismissing him was too lenient. We should still instruct the general manager to pursue the matter according to the law and thoroughly investigate the accomplices. On one hand, the supervisory committee should thoroughly investigate the company's business accounts to clarify the facts. The results of the review showed that all incoming and outgoing goods, as well as cloth坯 and printed cloth stored in the factory and warehouse, were clearly recorded and there was no mixing of enemy goods. Since your association sent personnel to investigate this case, it has been more than ten days and the truth should not be difficult to reveal. However, since the investigation, the case has been pending and all business has been suspended. Our board of directors and colleagues have painstakingly founded the Printing and Dyeing Company, originally to resist imported goods. We have never asked ourselves to be behind others in patriotism. How could we knowingly sell enemy goods? Moreover, the company's accounts must be audited by an accountant and reported to the shareholders' meeting. It is not allowed to operate enemy goods in addition to its own business. It is clear that this is not allowed by the circumstances. However, the company's organization of the board of directors only holds a supervisory position and does not bear actual executive responsibility, which has led to corrupt employees colluding and engaging in malpractice. This is truly intolerable by our association and deeply hated by all shareholders of our company. We are now pursuing the matter according to the law, and we will not tolerate any accomplices. We respectfully ask your association to uphold justice, adhere to the original intention of patriotism and support for commerce, and consider the national goods industry. We hereby announce the actual situation to all parties to clarify the facts and stop the rumors. We are deeply grateful. Sincerely, Shanghai Printing and Dyeing Company Board of Directors."

Commerce Section Report: Upon receiving the order to investigate whether the Shanghai Printing and Dyeing Company's products had been modified or counterfeited, we proceeded to conduct a detailed investigation. First, we inquired with the company about its organization, printing and dyeing procedures, and sales situation, and reviewed its books and verified its goods. Then, we investigated with the customer help line to find out how the goods were transacted with the company. The investigation results are listed below: (1) Regarding the company, on the 3rd of this month, together with Zhu and Li of the Cotton Cloth Industry Association, we went to the company's factory in Gaolang Bridge to investigate. The factory director, Mr. Wu, guided us to visit the machine room, workshop, and other places. It was divided into two departments, printing and dyeing, and the scale was quite large. There were more than 900 workers day and night, and a textile factory was under construction. It was said that all the cloth坯 in stock were ordered from Tianxiang, Jardine Matheson, Carlowitz, Shenxin, etc. We then cut six pieces of sample cloth, and the factory stamped each piece. After carefully examining the factory, no clues could be found. Then, we went to the company's distribution office, where we were met by the general manager, Zhang Rongchu. I asked him to read the account books, but due to the late hour, I did not have time to read them in detail. The company sent a page of clear accounts to the association, including the number of incoming and outgoing goods and inventory. The next day, we were ordered to extract 16 books from the company (including two copies of incoming ticket receipts, three copies of sales books, three copies of incoming books, two copies of silver books, two copies of silver rolling books, one copy of incoming goods book, and three copies of wholesale books). The next day, we went to extract the bank and money house transaction records. It was said that because the matter was important, we were asked to send someone to the company to review them. On the 8th of this month, we went to the company to extract eight customer account books and brought them back for joint review. After reviewing the company's incoming and outgoing goods accounts from September last year, we found that they were purchased from eight companies including Tianxiang. Except for Jianhua, whose factory had been destroyed and could not be investigated, after checking with Tianxiang, Jardine Matheson, Carlowitz, and Daqingfengda, they were all in compliance. Some of Shenxin's factory was handled by brokers and could not be verified. According to named and unnamed confidential reports, the factory's large flower wool silk cloth was changed in appearance. A letter was sent requesting to go to the factory to see him print it out. On the afternoon of the 16th of this month, we went to the factory and witnessed the factory workers printing a piece of flower cloth. The pattern and color were consistent with the sample from the confidential informant. There were a total of four of these patterns, and their copper roller numbers were 569, 563, 564, and 600. It was said that when the factory was opened, it originally used Japanese branch teachers. Since the Shenyang Incident, all the Japanese workers resigned one after another and were replaced by 13 Chinese people hired from the Lun Chang Company. Their skills were exquisite and superior to the Japanese, and their products were novel, which led to external doubts. (2) Information obtained from various parties: After investigating the company's internal affairs and reviewing various accounts, we found no traces of inferior goods being modified or counterfeited. Therefore, we changed our approach to investigating the customer help line that had dealings with the company, inspected the incoming goods book, and ordered a copy of the incoming goods account and the silver payment account. We found inconsistencies between the company's outgoing goods account and the silver receipt account. The quantity recorded on the incoming goods account and the silver payment account of each number was greater than the quantity recorded on the company's outgoing goods book. Even some customer homes did not have a transaction account name in the company's account, but later the customer's family actually had a record of receiving more than 50 boxes from the company. Only five investigations had exceeded 295 boxes and 2,240疋. Although the company's general manager, Zhang Rongchu, claimed that (1) because the silver period had not arrived and there were returns, the account had not been entered, (2) because brokers transferred the goods, the customer's name was not registered, but after investigation, first, most of the goods from each number had been paid for and receipts had been obtained; second, the customer's book registration was under the name of Shanghai Printing and Dyeing Company or Shanghai Factory, and there was no mention of anyone transferring the goods. This shows that Zhang Rongchu's words are not credible. Based on the above situation, it is proved that someone used the company's name and trademark to modify and counterfeit goods outside, hoping to obtain illegal profits, which is beyond doubt. Later, because of its organized actions and ingenious design, it was not easy to detect, which caused the customers who traded with the company to be blinded. Now, after investigation, it is naturally impossible to hide it. What should be studied at present is who is exercising the modification and counterfeiting, and who is responsible. The company's letter on August 8 stated that a runner, Zhou Yanqing, had set up an organization on Pingliang Road in July to transform enemy goods into the company's trademark and sell them in the market. The Yulin Road Police Station cracked down on it, and later, because of considering his poverty, he was not investigated deeply and only suspended his job and wrote a letter of repentance. However, the most that a runner can do is to steal the company's trademark. It is impossible to use the company's name. Now, it has been found that the floating goods are sold to each number under the company's name. This kind of organized behavior cannot be accomplished by a runner alone. According to Zhang Rongchu, Zhou Yanqing transformed the company's and Lun Chang Company's trademarks on Pingliang Road and was searched by the police station for more than 70疋. Zhou Yanqing compensated Lun Chang Company 5,000 yuan, etc. The company's letter also said that considering his poverty, he was not investigated deeply. How could a poor person be able to pay a fine of 5,000 yuan? This proves that Zhou Yanqing's counterfeiting of goods has someone else in charge. After this association discovered it, the company's general manager, Zhang Rongchu, did not deny the excess quantity in each number's incoming goods payment account, but only used untruthful excuses to try to cover it up. Therefore, Zhang Rongchu is highly suspected in this case. See the company's board of directors' letter on August 16, which vaguely states that the board of directors only has a supervisory position and does not bear actual executive responsibility, etc. Then, Zhang Rongchu, as the general manager, is in charge of the overall situation. What is his responsibility? It is also impossible to escape responsibility. The company's board of directors' letter stated that the company's accounts must be audited by an accountant and reported to the shareholders' meeting. It is not allowed to operate enemy goods in addition to its own business. After investigating the company, the general ledger for the first half of the year was indeed audited and stamped by an accountant. What they said is still true. Moreover, in the world, employees never give their gains to the public. Therefore, it is credible that the external modification and counterfeiting were not known in advance by the shareholders and board of directors of the company's main body. However, the user embezzled the company's name and engaged in corruption and malpractice, which violated the law. The letter also said that the matter is now being pursued according to the law, and all accomplices will not be tolerated. In order to implement the purpose of resisting goods and safeguard the legal interests of members, it seems that the company's board of directors should be responsible for thoroughly investigating Zhang Rongchu, who is highly suspected in this case, and all accomplices according to the law. The above sections are all factual investigations. Please review them and submit them to the Standing Committee for a ruling.

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce Telegram Pays Attention to Fictitious Factory Numbers and Trademarks 143

Send Personnel to Check Goods Upon Arrival

Detain Goods if Suspected

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce issued a special telegram yesterday due to the recent frequent occurrence of fictitious factory numbers and trademarks being used to transport and sell goods. The telegram stated: "To all national public organizations, our association has carefully examined the opinions of merchants and believes that the means used by unscrupulous merchants are nothing more than two: one is to send yarn and cloth to the factory for dyeing, because inferior yarn cannot be distinguished after dyeing; the other is to change the appearance, or falsely create domestic factory numbers, or imitate domestic trademarks, so as to confuse the goods. Therefore, even if they are inferior goods, they are sold in various places and are not easily detected for a while. Our association has previously decided to inform the dyeing factory by letter that it must not cut off the machine head during dyeing, which makes it difficult to identify, in order to prevent fraud. In addition, how to check and prevent fraud is still under discussion. As for the level of fictitious factory numbers and trademarks, we should ask your organizations to send personnel to check the goods upon arrival in the territory. If the brand number and trademark have never been sold or seen in your place before, you should immediately detain the goods in a public place and send a telegram to our association to inquire about the actual situation before releasing them, so as to be prudent and avoid malpractice. Signed, Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce."

The world-renowned Chinese technical master Mr. Landershan, along with Ms. Minanisha and other members of their troupe, embarked on the President McKinley (PresMakinley) ship for their fifth world tour. They will first perform in Los Angeles, USA, with an expected return in about three years.

Last Year's Chinese Overseas Trade

Overseas trade is of great importance, reflecting national strength and public sentiment, and cannot be ignored by those who discuss politics, economics, the nation, and society. Our country has consistently experienced a trade deficit, and people have been advocating for the promotion of domestic goods as a fundamental national strategy. However, the government lacks concrete plans, and the people lack unified organization. Empty talk is of no help. Let us examine the statistical figures of overseas trade. How can one not be alarmed and urgently seek improvement? Overseas trade must pass through customs, so the truth of overseas trade can be reliably discerned from customs statistics. This newspaper has specially consulted customs inspection reports, excerpting the most important aspects and presenting them here, so that the people can be vigilant.

The total value of foreign trade in the 20th year of the Republic of China, calculated in terms of silver, amounted to 234,300,000 Kuping taels. Broken down, imports were worth 143,400,000 taels, and exports were worth 90,900,000 taels, resulting in a trade deficit of 52,500,000 taels. Compared to the 19th year of the Republic of China, with imports of 131,000,000 taels and exports of 89,500,000 taels, resulting in a trade deficit of 41,500,000 taels, and the 18th year of the Republic of China, with imports of 126,600,000 taels and exports of 100,150,000 taels, resulting in a trade deficit of 15,100,000 taels, the situation is even worse. However, when calculated in US dollars, due to the rising gold price, the import value of 810,000,000 US dollars in the 18th year of the Republic of China and 603,000,000 US dollars in the 19th year of the Republic of China was only worth 488,800,000 US dollars in the 20th year.

Looking at imports and exports separately (in units of thousands of taels), in the 20th year, the most imports came from the United States, totaling 32,026,600 Kuping taels, followed by Japan with 29,038,600 taels, then Hong Kong with 21,817,000 taels, and then the United Kingdom with 11,934,400 taels. Compared to the 19th year, imports from the United States increased by 9,861,300 taels, imports from Japan decreased by 3,191,700 taels, imports from Hong Kong increased by 6,747,000 taels, and imports from the United Kingdom increased by 1,222,600 taels.

In the 20th year, the most exports went to Japan, valued at 26,495,600 Kuping taels, followed by Hong Kong with 14,831,200 taels, then the United States with 12,020,050 taels, and then the United Kingdom with 6,452,600 taels. Compared to the 19th year, exports to Japan increased by 4,840,100 taels, exports to Hong Kong decreased by 9,700,600 taels, exports to the United States decreased by 1,167,500 taels, and exports to the United Kingdom increased by 185,700 taels.

Chinese overseas trade extends across the globe, not just to the four places listed above. These four places are listed because their import and export volumes are the largest in value. In terms of trade surplus and deficit, in the 20th year of the Republic of China, the countries with a trade surplus were Siam with 168,000 taels, the Dutch East Indies with 7,526,000 taels, Persia and Egypt with 21,200,800 taels, Denmark with 2,311,000 taels, the Netherlands with 36,035,000 taels, France with 12,691,000 taels, Soviet Russia with 30,092,000 taels, and Korea with 195,000 taels. The countries with a trade deficit were the United States with 20,006,100 taels, Japan with 25,430,000 taels, Hong Kong with 69,858,000 taels, Macau with 888,000 taels, Annam with 8,970,000 taels, the Dutch East Indies with 41,214,000 taels, India with 66,871,000 taels, the United Kingdom with 54,818,000 taels, Norway with 1,490,000 taels, Sweden with 4,076,000 taels, Germany with 60,030,000 taels, Belgium with 26,185,000 taels, Switzerland with 4,124,000 taels, Italy with 10,637,000 taels, Canada with 18,836,000 taels, Cuba with 426,000 taels, South Australia with 59,544,000 taels, and other countries with 4,543,000 taels, totaling 524,013,000 taels (the previous table was in millions, hence the value of 525,000,000).

In conclusion, China's overseas trade is primarily with the United States, the United Kingdom, and Japan. Based on the situation in the 20th year, Japan's imports declined due to the boycott, with goods like yarn, cloth, sugar, coal, and seafood being hit. India fell to fourth place due to reduced rice imports of 8 million piculs. As for Germany, woolen goods, chemical industry products, steel, and paper all flourished. The United States saw a surge in exports of agricultural surpluses, such as cotton and wheat, with tobacco, timber, and gasoline also being significant. South Australia's main import was wheat.

The largest export was raw silk, sold to Japan, the United States, the United Kingdom, France, India, and other places. In the 20th year, 32,719 bales were sold to Japan, 29,741 bales to the United States, 18,805 bales to France, and 9,525 bales to India. The largest market for tea was Russia, with 240,824 bales sold, while Egypt, Turkey, and other places also accounted for 162,392 bales, with the United Kingdom and the United States taking far less. Soybeans were sold to Russia, Japan, the Netherlands, the United Kingdom, and other places, with 15 million piculs sold to Russia, 11 million piculs to Japan, 6 million piculs to the Netherlands, and 3 million piculs to the United Kingdom. The import trade situation in the 20th year of the Republic of China underwent even more changes than in previous years, making it difficult to exhaustively describe. This was due to the sharp drop in silver prices, unstable exchange rates, reduced purchasing power among the Chinese people, the boycott of Japanese goods, increased import taxes, overproduction in various countries, and reduced global demand. These factors led to increased competition for sales in China, resulting in falling prices. Chinese exports also fell due to the principle of import and export offsetting each other. Although exports increased relatively in the 20th year, imports still increased by 12.4 million compared to the 19th year.

The increase in imports and exports in the 20th year compared to the 19th year was largely due to the relationship between the value of gold and silver. Therefore, imports calculated in US dollars were actually nearly 200 million less than in the 19th year, as mentioned above. Furthermore, the majority of imports were surplus products from foreign countries. The following is a detailed list of the statistics for major imported goods over the past three years:

18th Year 19th Year 20th Year

(Thousands of Kuping Taels)

Cotton 91,124 132,266 179,082

Cotton Textiles 188,574 149,839 121,078

Wheat 12,421 12,831 87,639

Sugar 98,761 86,391 85,889

Minerals 70,855 75,881 85,123

Machine Oil/Gasoline 64,779 65,045 79,757

Rice 58,981 121,234 64,376

Tobacco 49,162 58,373 62,681

Machinery 29,887 44,283 43,605

Paints 33,192 25,765 39,441

Timber 27,819 23,178 34,685

Woolen Textiles 44,431 24,616 32,564

Flour 64,008 31,926 30,920

As seen from the above, imports have varied over the past three years. Machinery and machine oil are not produced domestically, so there is nothing to say. However, cotton, wheat, timber, and other items are mostly imported, even though our country is known as an agricultural nation. Furthermore, although the Chinese people have not ceased to research, study, and establish factories to manufacture chemicals, paints, and sugar, the comparison over the past three years shows that the import value has relatively increased due to the rise in gold prices. This demonstrates that the effectiveness of domestic goods is still limited. Given China's current poverty and the constant occurrence of natural and man-made disasters, yet each year there is a trade deficit of 400 to 500 million, the enormity of this amount over decades can be seen. If the Chinese people do not have the capacity to bear this burden, they will inevitably go bankrupt due to accumulation. At this time of increasing foreign aggression and efforts to survive, how should readers be inspired to seek salvation after seeing these few lines of statistics? This places a great responsibility on the Chinese people.

Local News Two

Heavy Rain Again in Our City Yesterday 145

Since the beginning of autumn, the weather has been extremely hot, leading to an increase in epidemics among the citizens, spreading most rapidly in the Wusong area. This is likely due to the prolonged drought. Over the past two days, the weather has been even more stifling, with the Fahrenheit thermometer reaching over 98 degrees. Even sitting still indoors, one feels perspiration pouring out, making one feel intoxicated. Yesterday afternoon, around 4:15, the temperature suddenly changed, and dark clouds gathered instantly, making it as dark as night. Soon after, lightning flashed, thunder roared, and torrential rain poured down, lasting for about an hour before slightly subsiding. The thunder and lightning also stopped, and a cool breeze followed, refreshing the mind. In areas with lower elevations in the Shanghai West Extra-Settlement Roads, such as Jessfield Road, Avenue Haig, Robison Road, and in the French Concession such as Rue du Marche, West Xinqiao, Rue de Consulat, and in the English Concession such as Foochow Road, Hankow Road, and Shantung Road, pedestrians were ankle-deep in water. The roads in Zhabei and the Nanshi area were also turned into swamps. The areas around the South Railway Station and the 16 Prefectures, being low-lying, experienced accumulated water forming channels due to insufficient drainage. Areas such as Gonghe Xin Road, Qujiang Road, near the Zha Bei dry bridge, Maigen Road Station, and Jiaotong Road were completely flooded. Commuters relied on rickshaws for transportation, causing rickshaw prices to skyrocket, with some fares reaching three to four jiao for very short distances. Some houses with lower elevations were flooded. This was the first heavy rain after the beginning of autumn. However, the wind stopped and the weather turned hot again in the evening, with occasional flashes of lightning, leading to more rain, though not as heavy. By 11:00 PM, it gradually thinned out and then stopped completely. This morning around 3:00 AM, the autumn breeze was cool, and those wearing only thin clothing felt slightly chilled.

Three Master Swindlers Set Up Eight Bogus Companies 146

Each Used Several Aliases

Fraudulently Signed Bad Checks

Defrauded Many Goods

Those Defrauded Can Report

Recently, a swindler surnamed Zhu, using five aliases: Jintang, Wenbin, Wenquan, Jianqiu, and Dajun, and his accomplice surnamed Chen, also using aliases such as Yongbao, Ronghui, Yu Chenbin, etc., colluded with Zhang Boqing to set up eight bogus foreign firms in various locations. Their addresses and registered numbers are as follows: (1) Baili Foreign Firm, 36 Sijing Road; (2) Shenhe Foreign Firm, Avenue Edward VII; (3) Weilu Foreign Firm, Sijing Road; (4) Changxin Tobacco Company, 451 North Jiangxi Road; (5) Jianfu Foreign Firm; (6) Jingchang Foreign Firm; (7) Hongdachang Company, 237 Yanging Lane, Xiamen Road; (8) Tongchangfeng Company, Yongan Street. Using very small amounts of money, they opened accounts at the American, Jin Cheng, Ken Yeh, and Hua Tong banks to obtain checkbooks and fraudulently obtained goods from various Chinese and foreign commercial firms and companies, which they then sold and divided the profits. This was recently exposed, and the General Inspectorate of Police was notified. Detectives were dispatched to arrest Zhu and his two accomplices. Upon initial investigation, it was found that eleven businesses, including the Daguangming Electrical Material Store on Ningbo Road, had been defrauded, with losses totaling about 2,000 gold. It is believed that there are more victims. Yesterday morning, the three master swindlers were handed over to the First Special District Local Court. Judge Liu conducted a preliminary hearing and ordered them to be detained for further investigation and a subsequent hearing. Those who have been defrauded but have not yet reported the case can directly submit a report to the police, truthfully stating the amount and type of loss, to be included in the investigation and punishment.

Workers at the Sanyou Factory Continued Their Hunger Strike Yesterday 150

Various Parties Sent Representatives to Offer Condolences

Food Allowances Were Still Not Received Yesterday

The General Labor Union Petitioned the Municipal Government Yesterday

After twenty-three workers, including Hong Jiaben, at the main factory of the Sanyou Industrial Company in Yinxianggang began their hunger strike the day before, the crying for help delegation continued to run around and appeal to various parties yesterday. The workers' food allowances have still not been received. The details are recorded below.

Continued Hunger Strike After twenty-three workers, including Hong Jiaben, at the Sanyou Factory began their hunger strike the day before yesterday, they remained lying in the factory's low-quality gauze rooms yesterday. Having not consumed a grain of rice or a drop of water for over a day and night, they were extremely exhausted. In order to protect the workers' lives, the Seventh District Cotton Textile Industry Labor Union repeatedly urged them to eat. However, all the workers continued their hunger strike from morning till night yesterday.

Condolences from Various Parties After the workers at the Sanyou Factory began their hunger strike, various parties were moved upon hearing the news. Those who visited to offer condolences yesterday included representatives from the First District Shipbuilding Labor Union, the Steamboat Woodworking Labor Union, Ye Xianggao, the Electricity Company Labor Union, Wang Han, the Road Industry Labor Union, Ren Jieting, Chen Hanzhang, the Postal Workers Labor Union, Cao Chongye, the Steamboat Stewards Labor Union, Ye Gonglun, the Mercerizing and Dyeing Industry Labor Union, Liu Jintai, Lu Muqin, the Sixth District Water and Electricity Labor Union, Li Yongxiang, and the Municipal Party Headquarters also sent Committee Member Lu Jingshi to offer condolences. The representatives brought various foods such as fruits and milk and urged the workers to eat, but the workers remained determined and refused to eat. Later, doctors determined that Hong Jiaben, Zhang Zegang, Shen Yucheng, and three others were showing signs of illness and needed immediate treatment. The Seventh District Cotton Textile Industry Labor Union was immediately notified to transport the three to the Shanghai West Labor Hospital for treatment.

Petition to the General Committee On the matter of the hunger strike by the workers at the Sanyou Factory, General Labor Union Committee members Zhu Xuefan, Shao Xubai, Yu Xianting, and Li Mengnan went to the Municipal Government to petition at 10:00 AM yesterday. Secretary-General Yu received them, and the representatives presented three points: (1) Please send a special commissioner from the Municipal Government to be responsible for handling the Sanyou Factory incident immediately; (2) Order the management to resume operations within a limited time; (3) If any unfortunate incidents occur due to the workers' hunger strike, the management should be fully responsible. Secretary-General Yu replied that the first point would be handled immediately, and the second point would be handled according to the three measures previously decided by the Municipal Government, ordering the management to comply. If the management continues to resist, the Municipal Government will have to enforce them strictly. The third point is a legal issue and will be subject to legal sanctions, and the Municipal Government is not in a position to reply. The representatives were satisfied and then departed.

Food Not Issued The workers' temporary food allowance of 120 yuan per day was originally scheduled to be issued every Wednesday. However, over the past two days, representatives from party and government organizations, together with representatives from the labor union, have approached the management for the money, but the management has avoided meeting them, resulting in the money not being received. Yesterday morning, representatives from the labor union, together with Zhou Lianze, a representative from the Municipal Party Headquarters, Zhu Guilin, a representative from the Bureau of Social Affairs, and Dong Zhihe, a representative from the Public Security Bureau, went to the company again to collect the money. However, the company remained adamant and refused to change its position. Finally, it stated that whether or not a solution was reached, this would be the last payment. If they wanted to receive it, the representatives from the three party, government, and police organizations had to be responsible for signing. The three representatives refused on the spot, so the money was still not received.

British Public Bus Workers Petitioned the Municipal Government Yesterday 151

The Municipal Government Indicated Acceptance

The General Assembly Decided to Fight to the Death

The strike by the workers of the British Public Bus Company has now entered its ninth day, and the situation remains serious, with no hope of resolution. Yesterday morning, all the workers went to the Municipal Government to petition. In the afternoon, they held another general assembly and decided to fight to the death. Details are provided below. Petition Yesterday morning, over 200 striking public bus workers, all wearing yellow company uniforms, gathered in Caojiadu, lined up, and marched to the Municipal Government to petition. They arrived at the Municipal Government around 9:00 AM. Due to the large number of people, fearing incidents, the Public Security Bureau dispatched over 20 police officers to maintain order, so the situation was quite good. Representatives Shi Baoshan, Wang Xingmao, Zhang Bolin, Yuan Weixin, Chen Yuting, and five others were selected. As Secretary-General Yu was attending a meeting, Wang Shaozhai, the director of the Second Section of the Municipal Government, received them. The representatives first recounted the circumstances of the strike and requested that the Municipal Government mediate promptly. Director Wang indicated acceptance and promised to convey the message to the mayor and negotiate with the company. The workers lined up and left around noon.

Continued General Assembly After petitioning the Municipal Government yesterday, all the workers convened a general assembly at a location on Bailinan Road, with over 200 people in attendance. The presidium reported on the petition to the Municipal Government, and the crowd expressed their determination to fight to the death. Several important proposals were also discussed, but due to the importance of the matter, they were not announced.

Breaking the Water Tank At 4:00 PM yesterday, a Route 2 bus was passing near Bazilu when it was struck by striking workers with rocks, breaking the water tank. The bus could not continue to operate, and one passenger was injured in the head. The passenger hired a rickshaw to go to the hospital for treatment. Furthermore, a Route 9 bus was driving to the intersection of Pingliang Road in Yangshupu when striking workers threw an empty watermelon filled with fecal liquid into the bus, causing a foul odor to spread. As a result, the number of passengers on all routes has decreased.

Workers' Statement According to a statement issued by the Strike Committee, since the labor unrest occurred, because the company firmly rejected the workers' demands, the public was outraged, and a third party took advantage of the situation, resulting in actions outside the scope of the strike. A thorough investigation is now underway, and a report has been submitted to party and government organizations for investigation. The committee's future actions will be on the right track, waiting for the party and government organizations and various legal entities to uphold justice and mediate to seek a legitimate solution. The committee cannot be held responsible for any actions taken by third parties.

The Great Alliance for Promoting National Products Held a Factory Representatives' Congress Yesterday 154

The Shanghai Great Alliance for Promoting National Products held its fourth National Products Factory Representatives' Congress at the City General Chamber of Commerce yesterday afternoon at 4:00 PM. The purpose was to support the prohibition of the sale of Yaple light bulbs in Southeast Asia. Chairman Chen Yiting reported the purpose of the meeting, stating that the Yaple Electric Factory had been operating diligently and achieved considerable success in promoting overseas sales and reclaiming rights. Unexpectedly, it was subject to the Dutch company Philips' pretext of patent rights and a ban on the sale of glass tube pumping in Southeast Asia. This case is related to the future of national products and has a significant impact. The purpose of today's meeting is to discuss rescue measures, etc. Subsequently, Wang Jie'an, Sun Daosheng, and others expressed their opinions, and then resolutions were immediately passed: (1) To convene a city-wide public organization to form a committee to guarantee overseas trade in national products, and the selection and number of people will be handled by the Great Alliance; (2) To notify the factories belonging to this association to voluntarily refuse to use Philips light bulbs, and to send a letter to the National Electrical Industry Association to pay attention; (3) To telegraph the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to lodge a serious protest with the Dutch government and to review the company's patent for wave tube pumping. After the case was discussed, it was also resolved: (1) To notify all factories to enthusiastically respond to the call for exhibits from the representative of the Chicago Exposition Preparatory Office for national products and the Shandong National Products Exhibition Hall of the Ministry of Industry; (2) To notify all members to resolutely boycott Japanese goods; (3) To petition the municipal government to protect national products factories; (4) To petition the municipal government to provide relief for the heavy losses suffered by the Sanyou Baoye Society in the Shanghai war. The meeting adjourned at six o'clock.

Shanghai Machinery Association Statement 155

The Shanghai Machinery-Made National Products Factory Federation, located on Bellows Road, sent a letter stating: "To whom it may concern, the factory association has been organized for six years, and its purpose has always been to revitalize industry and promote national products. It is especially sympathetic to the boycott of enemy goods, and its achievements are obvious and have long been known. Since the September 18th Incident, in view of the violence of Japan and the urgency of national crisis, industry is related to the foundation of the country. Without concerted efforts and the use of domestic raw materials, there is no way to save the country. We have repeatedly sent letters to all member factories to strictly comply with this, and not to buy or sell inferior goods to provide the enemy with supplies. The facts are there and can be reviewed. Unexpectedly, recently, a group calling itself the 'Chinese Skull Punishing Traitors Corps' sent a letter to the association, stating that a certain factory had privately imported enemy goods. For the sake of the reputation of national products, please investigate and punish them quickly, etc. The righteousness is stern, and the enthusiasm for safeguarding national products is evident on paper. The association's duties lie within, and it should conduct a thorough investigation for review. However, the factory mentioned in the letter

only lists the factory name without distinguishing its nature. There are thousands of factories, large and small, in Shanghai, and only over two hundred have joined the association as members. It is difficult to distinguish between factories with the same name but different types. What kind of factory is mentioned in the group's letter? Is it a member of the association? What kind of enemy goods were imported? When and where were they purchased? All of these require detailed investigation. Unfortunately, the letter does not specify any of this, making it impossible to start. However, the association will still conduct a strict investigation of the factories with the same name as those mentioned in the letter among its members, in order to get to the bottom of the matter. On the other hand, it will also universally notify all members to strictly use domestic raw materials. It is also hoped that if patriotic groups have any reports in the future, please

provide accurate evidence to facilitate the investigation. Since the letter has no address, it is impossible to reply. We dare to borrow the newspaper to express our sincere advice and make a solemn statement to our patriotic compatriots, hoping for your clear observation. What is the matter? Shanghai Machinery-Made National Products Factory Federation kowtows and prints."

Letter Requesting that all City Students be Ordered to Wear Western Suits Made of Domestic Materials 157

Letter from the National Products Promotion Association to the Municipal Education Bureau

Zhang Qingfa and Zhang Dezai, executive members of the Shanghai Citizens' National Products Promotion Association, deeply regret that students in various schools wear Western suits, the raw materials of which are all imported, resulting in the outflow of rights and interests. The trends followed by the nation originate from what is observed, so they specifically proposed at the 26th regular meeting of the association to send a letter to the Municipal Education Bureau, ordering schools under its jurisdiction to promote national products and wear Western suits made of domestic raw materials, in order to correct perceptions and save the country. The letter is recorded as follows: (Omitted above) The association's 12th session, 26th regular meeting, Executive Member Zhang Qingfa and Executive Member Zhang Dezai proposed that a letter be sent to the Municipal Education Bureau to strictly order students in schools under its jurisdiction to wear clothing made of domestic materials. The matter was resolved to be handled as proposed and recorded. Shanghai is the center of national morality. The clothing of students above junior high school is mostly Western suits, and the clothing materials are all foreign goods. The loss of rights and interests is extremely large, hindering the national products movement. Moreover, students are the future masters of the country, and the trends followed by the nation originate from what is observed. The association promotes national products as its duty, and is unable to remain silent out of heartache. Therefore, in accordance with the proposal, a letter is sent to your esteemed bureau director, with the enthusiasm of maintaining national products, to strictly instruct the principals of all schools under your jurisdiction to supervise all students to uniformly wear Western suits made of domestic clothing materials, in order to correct perceptions and save the country. We also request that national universities be advised to do the same. The national economy and people's livelihood deeply depend on it. (Omitted below) We also telegraph the Ministry of Education in the capital to strictly order all schools nationwide to use national products for all needed items, except for those with no substitutes, and to order all students nationwide to wear clothing made of domestic raw materials, in order to demonstrate promotion and reverse the declining trend. (Similar wording omitted)

Disputes over Epidemic Inspection of the Xinfeng Ship 162

The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Xinfeng ship arrived on the 25th of last month and had a dispute with the seaway quarantine office, which was reported earlier. Later, the quarantine office forced the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company to punish the ship's chief mate, Jiang Changqing, which aroused the public anger of all the crew members of the Shanghai merchant ships. Yesterday, they sent a letter to the seaway quarantine office, stating that if the quarantine doctors do not comply with the regulations and quarantine outside the port, and if the doctors do not arrive on the ship at the specified time, then the future disputes will inevitably increase. In the future, all losses of passengers, crew members, and ships caused by this shall be borne by the quarantine office. The original letter was sent out yesterday. The general content is recorded as follows:

"To whom it may concern, we received a letter on the 27th of last month with a report in the newspaper. Everything was accurate, but your correction was completely inconsistent. The letter from the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's General Manager Li was also not the main cause of the dispute. Chief Mate Jiang Changqing of Xinfeng is a member of this association. This time, he was unexpectedly slandered. Xinfeng arrived at the Jinliyuan Wharf at 8:40 AM on July 25th. Dr. Qi arrived on the ship at 9:10 AM, half an hour later. All the passengers had already disembarked. The correction letter stated that the doctor arrived at the ship at 8:45 AM and was not absent from duty. This statement is completely inaccurate. According to the time Xinfeng arrived at the wharf and the time the medical officer arrived on the ship, as pointed out by the association, are both recorded in the old gram book signed by the shipowner, and stamped and signed by the Maritime Affairs Bureau and the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's chief shipowner. Your office wants to use this to cover up the absence from duty, but it is just enough to confirm the matter. Moreover, Xinfeng had hundreds of passengers. How could they all leave the ship in five minutes? Even if your office wants to erase the facts, it is too contradictory. Your office also claimed that Chief Mate Jiang accused the medical officer of causing trouble with the quarantine, so he raised the flag to summon the police to suppress the order. This is a lie. Since the doctor was half an hour late, the passengers had already left and there was no epidemic to examine. It was not necessary for Chief Mate Jiang to point out the trouble. The medical officer rebuked Chief Mate Jiang for not keeping the passengers, and Jiang retorted. The doctor became angry, summoned foreign police to take advantage of the situation to detain the ship, and deliberately harassed the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, forcing it to punish Chief Mate Jiang, abusing his power, wantonly threatening, and disrupting security. He did not want to issue a permit and did not allow Xinfeng to clear customs. He made a big fuss. The hidden situation is not worth asking deeply. Fortunately, the Business Bureau tolerated it and did not want to cause trouble, so it apologized to settle the matter. Your office is shameless and arrogant. As for praising the shipowners of various countries, it is especially a matter of unworthy people, who generate themselves outside, pick up other people's spit, to pursue private interests, and promote the West and suppress the Chinese, which has become the heart method of ancestors. I won't discuss the others. Regarding the quarantine of the Nagasaki Maru ship recently, he publicly refused, and the situation was ten times more serious than Xinfeng. However, the doctor was not seen summoning the police to suppress the order, maintaining order, and your office was not seen not issuing a permit because it did not hang the epidemic flag, and detaining the ship. As for the crew members, there was no request for punishment. The so-called praise and obedience of shipowners from various countries is really a decoration of the facade, which is suitable to show its ugliness. Is it true that we should be fair in everything, regardless of Chinese or foreign, and stick to it? Even if this association does not say it, how can the public opinion of society escape? Moreover, there is something else to be said. Unanimity against foreign countries, cooperation in strength, and avoidance of internal strife have always been my wishes. However, according to the general practice in various places, the quarantine of seagoing vessels is carried out outside the port, so as to prevent its spread. Only your office has created a new example, not only carrying it out in the port, but even on the dock. Regardless of whether this

method is stipulated in the regulations, it is ultimately not appropriate in practice, which can be asserted. According to Shanghai port, due to various reasons, navigation is very difficult. The crew members bear the responsibility for the safety of the lives and property of a ship. From the time of entry to the time of stopping, the authority of the driver in terms of driving is absolutely not allowed to be directed by the epidemic doctor again. Therefore, the quarantine of this port, Wusong port, has a specified location where it anchors for inspection, which is also LuarantieAnchorag. For decades, it has been inconvenient to engage in it. Now we have taken back the self-management, and increased the country

international status as the banner, then we should follow the good and follow the progress, and we should not hinder people with difficult methods due to our own inability to strive for progress. If this is not changed for a long time, there will be more places to cause disputes in the future. Such incidents are also related to changing the location. Moreover, your office claims to be handling quarantine in accordance with navigation practices. It is better to be silent, which is not the purpose of a gentleman loving others with virtue, but to see the detachment of right and wrong, and to leave hidden worries for the world and the hearts of people. Moreover, this association has more to declare. In the future, if the quarantine is not carried out outside the port and the doctor's arrival time on the ship is not specified, then all damages to passengers, ships, crew members, etc. caused by

Page 16

this should be borne by your office. Please pay attention to avoid shirking responsibility afterwards. This is a letter of reply. I hope you will check and take note of it. Shanghai Merchant Ship Drivers' Association."

Liu Gao's Mother and Son Were Burned by the Fire

At 1:25 AM this morning, a fire suddenly broke out downstairs in the house of a man named Liu from Changshu in Wenfu

Lane, Shangwen Road, Xiaoximen. Because it was late at night, everyone in the house was asleep, so they did not notice the fire when it started. Prohibition of Shirtless Sleeping in the Open 164

Joint Announcement by the Public Security and Health Bureaus

The Municipal Public Security and Health Bureaus jointly issued an announcement yesterday, saying: "For the purpose of the announcement, it is found that it is the time of the hot summer, and epidemics are easy to occur. Recently, it has been found that citizens take off their shirts to cool off during the day everywhere, and there are even more people sleeping in the open at night. The First Route of the Chinese Public Bus will be Restored 165

The Shanghai Chinese Public Bus Company, after the end of the Shanghai War, except for the third route [that is, the Zhabei to Zhenru resumed traffic, the rest, such as the Jiangwan first route, was delayed due to the Japanese soldiers stationed here, and the Yokohama Road Bridge in that area was bombed, and the traffic was blocked. Gambling Den Busted on White Earl Road 166

Detectives Li Yousheng and Liu Kun, detectives Kong Qing Tong, Bai Xiuzheng, Zhang Dongcheng, and others from the French Concession police station discovered that a Cantonese man named Wu Ajiang had recently set up a gambling den in Building 15, Taihe Lane, White Earl Road, to lure and deceive rural people into gambling. At 5:15 PM the day before yesterday, they went to the gambling den and arrested the boss Wu Ajiang, the lookout Chen Nanbing, the dealers Yang Bingquan and Gu Linlong, and the gamblers Xu Dexi, Wu Amao, and Zhang Yousheng, totaling seven people. They also seized over twenty gambling dollars, a piece of magnetite, three sets of dice, two hundred and forty chips, a piece of painted cloth, several raised boards, and seven notebooks, and brought them all back to the police station. He asked for verification. Wu confessed that he did not know he was tearing the seal by mistake and begged for forgiveness. Judge Zhang announced the end of the debate. Wu Ajiang and Wu Amao were returned to custody. Chen Nanbing, Yang Bingquan, and Gu Linlong were released on bail. Xu Deshan and Zhang Yousheng were ordered to post twenty yuan in cash bail and wait for sentencing.

Thirty-Two Yuan Each in the Hangzhou Area

In order to arouse the public's interest in air travel, China Aviation Corporation has specially prepared air tours for people from all walks of life to take for a short period of time. Now it has been prepared and is divided into two areas: (1) The Shanghai-Songjiang area, including Wusong and the sky around Shanghai; (2) The Hangzhou area, including the sky over Hangzhou City. Yesterday, letters were sent to the Garrison Command, the Municipal Government, and the Hangzhou Municipal Government for inspection. The ride method is as follows: (1) Shanghai-Songjiang area: each plane can seat five people, fifteen yuan per person, circling the city of Shanghai in the sky for about twenty-five minutes. A single package is seventy yuan. (2) Hangzhou area: each five-seater plane from Shanghai to Hangzhou requires one hundred and sixty yuan, thirty-two yuan per person, and it will only depart when it is full of five people. Round trip will be charged additionally. Fly to Hangzhou in the morning and return to Shanghai in the afternoon. Those who go to Hangzhou for sightseeing can also land at West Lake. It is scheduled to be implemented next week.

Fire Administration in the Public Concession in July 169

The Director of the Fire Administration of the Municipal Council reported in July that a total of sixty-eight fire alarms were received this month. Excluding false alarms and special summonses, there were actually fifty-two fire alarms. Due to the fire, property was endangered for a total of more than four million taels, but the actual loss was only more than twenty-three thousand taels. Five firefighters were injured in the fire this month, and eighteen others were injured, including eleven who were injured in special events. Firefighters on duty in entertainment venues totaled 11,326 hours.

The most serious fire in July was the one that occurred on the 12th at the intersection of North Suzhou Road and North Fujian Road. Because the report was delayed, the Hongkou Fire Brigade arrived on the scene when the fire was already raging. Because the wind was strong, the fire was feared to spread, so the central district was notified to send a team to assist. After rescue from all sides, the fire was extinguished after one hour and twenty minutes. It is estimated that one house was completely destroyed, three houses suffered significant losses, and four houses were affected.

The emergency team of the ambulance team received a total of 198 calls in July, which is the highest number of calls in a month since its establishment in January last year. From the beginning of January to the end of July this year, there were a total of 855 calls, compared with 439 calls in the same period last year. In July this year, the number of people rescued was 51 people who had accidents on the road, 36 people with acute illnesses, 31 people in fights, 25 people with heatstroke, 7 people with opium poisoning, 6 people who committed suicide, 4 people who collapsed suddenly, 3 people who were burned by fire, 3 people with knife wounds, 3 people who drowned, 1 person who was poisoned, 1 person who was shot, 3 people with unknown causes, and 41 other people, for a total of 215 people, including 45 women. Also, the hospital team received a total of 297 calls this month, and transported 348 patients in and out of the hospital.

Apprentice Beaten by Master, Case Involves Litigation 170

Shi Zhang, a woman from Rugao, alleges that her son, Shi Sanwangzi, thirteen years old this year, became a copper apprentice at the Huang Bao Car Shop owned by Sun Xingyu, a native of Taixing, located at No. 5 and 6, Lujiabang, Haichao Temple in the South City, in March of this year. Unexpectedly, on the 11th of this month, Shi Sanwangzi suddenly died. Shi Zhang filed a complaint with the local court yesterday, stating that according to her neighbor, Xu Zhongmei, on the 9th of this month, her son ate an apple, which led Sun to tie his hands and feet and use iron chopsticks to pry them, forcing him to confess to theft. Subsequently, he was severely beaten with a car shaft. When the police arrived to intervene, Sun claimed he was punishing his own son, so the police did not interfere. However, the child died from his injuries on the 11th. Sun immediately bribed neighbors Ye Jiu'er and Xiaozhu'er to secretly collect and enshroud the body at 9 PM that night, abandoning the coffin in the eastern part of the Yi Tomb grounds. He even wrote Sun Jinsheng on the coffin, intending to pass him off as his own son to cover up the traces of abuse leading to death. However, the police station refused, so he bribed doctor Yang Yuzhai to forge a medical certificate to register with the household registration at the police station, showing extreme malice. However, a human life is of paramount importance and must be investigated. It is requested that an autopsy be performed after exhumation.

Trial of Robbers Repeatedly Committing Robberies 171

The robbers Zhang Jinbiao, Zhu Jilin, Shen Kunfa, and Wang Shunde, between July 31st and the 16th of this month, gathered a gang and robbed Wang Shungui at No. 71, Xinjili, Dengtuo Road, and Chen Guisheng at No. 111, Mingyuanfang, Huade Road, stealing clothing and silver dollars worth over eight hundred yuan. They were subsequently arrested by Cai Zhitian, a Chinese detective inspector from the Huishan Police Department, and detective Ma Wenda. They confiscated a handgun and nine bullets, and confessed that the handgun was purchased from Bao Genxiang, residing at No. 55, Zhangjiazhai, Zhabei. The detectives arrested Bao and took him into custody at the police station. Yesterday morning, they were escorted to the Fourth Criminal Court of the First Special District Court. Zhang Tianyin, the police lawyer, stated that the case originated when Zhang Jinbiao saw a woman carrying a child and a bag on Broadway Road the day before. She was about to board a certain tram when Zhang stole her bag and fled. He was later apprehended by police detectives on Ayer Coke Road. The next morning, he was sent to the court, where he spoke to the second defendant, Zhu Jilin, near the court, acting suspiciously. When asked if they were accomplices, they claimed to be involved in the robbery of the Chen family on Huade Road. Zhu then implicated the third defendant, Shen Kunfa, residing at No. 8, Chenjiaxiang, Hongzhen. When the police went to arrest him, Zhu said he feared he would be overheard by the detectives in the courthouse. They took Zhu along to point out Shen, and successfully found a handgun and nine bullets in a pot under a bamboo fence in Shen's home. Shen also confessed that the handgun was purchased from Bao Genxiang at No. 55, Zhangjiazhai, Zhabei. The police again arrested Bao. Currently, the above two robbery cases are under investigation. The victims have arrived to identify the defendants, and the handgun, bullets, a gold watch, two pearls, and several articles of clothing, which are part of the original stolen goods, have been presented for inspection. According to the victim Wang Zhangshi (Wang Shungui's wife), the defendants Zhang, Zhu, and Shen were all present and robbed her of the gold watch and pearls, which were all original stolen goods. According to Chen Zhangshi, Chen Guisheng stated that Zhang, Shen, and Wang were the robbers present at the scene, etc. After Judge Fu Lin questioned each defendant, he ordered them to be remanded in custody for further investigation and trial.

Record of the General Meeting of the Yarn, Socks, and Dyeing Trade Association 178

The Shanghai Yarn, Socks, and Dyeing Trade Association held a general membership meeting at the Youth Propaganda Group yesterday. Fifty-four representatives from various factories attended. Shi Zhifang, Li Wentai, Tong Baorun, and others were publicly elected as the presidium. After the formalities were completed, the association's secretary, Wang Lixian, reported on the purpose of the meeting and the association's past activities. Then, Li Ruzhang, a representative from the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, gave a speech, urging all factories to refuse to use Japanese goods. His words were full of warning. After that, various proposals were discussed: (1) Regarding the industry regulations submitted to the Social Bureau for approval, a resolution was passed that everyone should abide by them. (2) Regarding the uniform dyeing prices for the industry, there was considerable debate at the time. As a result, it was resolved that the secretariat should modify the existing regulations and submit them to the Social Bureau and Municipal Chamber of Commerce for record-keeping before implementation. (3) Regarding the refusal to dye Japanese goods and the refusal to use Japanese raw materials, it was resolved that everyone should refuse to dye and use them, and that the Japanese goods inspection team should resume its work. (4) Regarding the standard for collecting membership fees, it was resolved that the fee should be collected in five grades: 2 yuan, 4 yuan, 6 yuan, 8 yuan, and 10 yuan. Tea and snacks were then served, and the meeting adjourned at 7 PM.

Letter to the Editor 184

To the Editor:

After reading the daily news columns of your esteemed newspaper on August 17th regarding the import of Japanese paper in July, totaling 1,180+ pieces and occupying the first place, we are providing a summary of the true situation of the foreign paper industry below for inclusion in your letter to the editor column in order to clarify the situation: (1) Before the September 18th Incident, the import of foreign paper into Shanghai was about 20,000 pieces per month, of which Japanese paper accounted for 50%. (2) After the September 18th Incident, the sales of Japanese paper plummeted. The import of 1,180+ pieces of Japanese paper in July is indeed a small number, accounting for less than 10%. The claim that it occupied the first place is a misunderstanding. (3) Most of the aforementioned imported Japanese paper was directly resold to Hankou and Tianjin by Japanese merchants. (4) Sales of foreign paper are still dominated by Western goods. Although there are Japanese merchants running around and unscrupulous individuals selling to various users, the number is extremely small.
